The Mighty Avengers offered three structural features the subject had not been offered before in combination: (1) a Black-led, Black-majority operational frame, in which he was not the only or the unusual presence; (2) a community-protective rather than category-eradicative mission, which invited him to *guard* rather than only to *hunt*; (3) a leadership cadre — Cage in particular — who did not require him to perform tactical justification for his methods. He was, briefly and visibly, *less guarded.* The record shows him in the team kitchen. The record shows him in the team kitchen *more than once.* Artists draw him in this era with the coat unbuttoned. The semiotic weight of that, given the prior forty years of buttoned-to-the-collarbone depiction, is substantial.

The experiment did not last. The team's editorial dissolution coincided with Secret Wars and the post-Secret Wars reshuffling, and the subject reverted to itinerant mode. But Phase B established something that Phases C and D would build on: *he is capable of integration into a civic frame when that frame is constructed in a register that does not require him to suppress the racial and historical specificity of his existence.* Prior teams had treated him as a tactical asset who happened to be Black; the Mighty Avengers treated him as a member of a community who happened to be a tactical asset. The distinction is the entire difference, and his nervous system registered it.

---

### Phase C: Mystical Stratification and the Strange-Adjacent Period (circa 2016 – 2021)

Beginning around the Aaron *Doctor Strange* run and intensifying through Cates, MacKay, and into Spurrier's *Death of Doctor Strange: Blade* (2022), the subject is increasingly pulled into the mystical stratum of the Marvel operational ecology. The pattern is consistent: when Strange is unavailable, compromised, or dead, the supernatural-defense lattice of the planet defaults to a small handful of practitioners, and the subject is one of them. He has become, without seeking it, a *senior figure in mystical infrastructure.*

This is significant because it represents the first sustained period in which his decades of acquired occult knowledge — accreted in the craftsman-not-scholar manner described in the psychological workup — are *socially recognized* by the relevant peer community. He is consulted. He is deferred to on specific subdomains (vampirology, blood-magic, certain pre-Christian European folkloric mechanics). He does not seem to enjoy this recognition, but he does not refuse it.

The *Death of Doctor Strange: Blade* one-shot is the keystone document of Phase C and warrants close examination. With Strange dead, the subject is called upon to defend the body and to navigate the immediate magical succession crisis. The story foregrounds his loneliness within the role: he is competent at the task and entirely without the apparatus — apprentices, sanctum, library, familiar — that a sorcerer accumulates. He performs the duty and walks away. The image at the close is structurally identical to the image at the close of any prior solo job across fifty years: a back, a coat, a doorway. The continuity of that image across decades and across registers (street-level vampirism to cosmic-mystical succession) is itself the central finding.

Concurrent with the mystical stratification, Phase C also contains:

- **The *Strikeforce* run (Tini Howard, 2019–2020).** Affiliation with a small clandestine cell (Spider-Woman, Wiccan, Hellstrom, Spectrum, Angela, Winter Soldier) focused on threats below the Avengers' visibility horizon. The team's brief lifespan and the subject's role within it — quiet, lethal, parental toward Wiccan in a way the page does not name but the panel composition makes plain — fit the pattern. He attaches to the youngest and most magically gifted member, mentors without speaking of mentorship, and exits when the cell collapses.
- **Ongoing intermittent guest work** in *Avengers*, *Strange Academy*, and adjacent titles. Strange Academy in particular shows him in fleeting paternal mode with adolescent practitioners; he is repeatedly drawn watching from doorways.

The unifying behavioral signature of Phase C is *increasing visibility paired with unchanged interiority.* He is seen more, by more people, in more rooms, and discloses nothing additional.

---

### Phase D: The Bryan Hill *Blade* Run and the Bright Cliff (2023 – 2024)

The most recent solo run reframes him at the operational scale he has been quietly occupying: planetary, mystical-political, and openly weary. Without recapitulating plot beats in detail, the run's diagnostic content is:

- **Confirmation that he has, by this point, killed more vampires than any living entity** and that this fact is known to the vampiric polity, which treats him as a category of weather rather than an individual adversary. The implications for his self-concept are unexamined within the text but are visible on the page: he carries the knowledge that his name is itself a deterrent, and he uses it as a tool while showing no satisfaction in possessing it.
- **A pronounced thematic emphasis on inheritance and lineage** — the Brooks name, the question of what is left after him, the existence of a daughter (Bloodline / Brielle Brooks, introduced in the *Bloodline: Daughter of Blade* limited series and the *Free Comic Book Day* materials, now active in *Bloodline*). The introduction of Brielle is the single most consequential development in the file's recent window and is treated separately below.
- **Tactical degradation under sustained mystical-political load.** The run shows him making errors he would not have made in the Wolfman era — misreading allies, overcommitting to fronts, accepting wounds he could have slipped. The errors are not catastrophic and are within the envelope of a seasoned operator under unusual pressure, but they are *errors*, and the file notes them. He is not aging in the chronological sense; the dhampir metabolism continues to present him as a man in his mid-thirties. He is aging in the *operational* sense — accumulating a fatigue that the body cannot metabolize because the body is not the locus of the fatigue.

---

### Phase E: The Daughter — Brielle Brooks (*Bloodline*, 2022 – present)

The discovery and integration of Brielle Brooks — daughter, dhampir by inheritance, adolescent, civilian-raised by her mother, untrained — is the most psychologically disruptive event in the subject's recent history and possibly in his entire post-Afari life. The file's analysis:

The existence of a biological child reorganizes every prior structural finding without contradicting any of them. He had constructed an existence on the assumption that the line ended with him — that the chimerism was a singular accident, that the Brooks lineage was operationally terminal, that the wound he carried was not transmissible. He was wrong on every count. Brielle inherits the metabolic anomaly. She inherits the predator-screening sensorium. She inherits, by accident of birth, a version of the founding wound — not perinatal maternal loss, but perinatal paternal absence, which in his case is genealogically and morally the same wound rotated ninety degrees.

His observable responses across the *Bloodline* materials are diagnostically rich:

- **Initial avoidance.** He does not, on first knowledge, present himself. He surveils. He confirms. He calibrates. This is the operational reflex; it is also a defense against the affective magnitude of the disclosure.
- **A protective register that exceeds his usual envelope.** When he does engage, the protective behavior is *visibly different in kind* from his protective behavior toward Faiza or toward Wiccan. It is grimmer. It is more frightened. He is more willing to threaten the world on her behalf than he has ever been willing to threaten it on his own.
- **A pedagogical instinct he has not previously demonstrated.** He attempts, awkwardly and with mixed results, to *teach.* The instruction is craft-level (weapons, scenting, restraint) rather than emotional, which is consistent with his lifelong cognitive style, but the attempt itself is unprecedented. He has been Afari to others before, in fragments (Faiza, Wiccan, certain Strange Academy adolescents). He has never been a father.
- **Recurrent self-doubt regarding the appropriateness of his own presence in her life.** This is the closest the canon has come to depicting him in something like ordinary moral self-examination. He does not journal. He does not speak the doubt aloud at length. But the panel-level beats — hesitations on thresholds, calls not made, gifts assembled and not delivered — are everywhere in the recent record.

The integration is unfinished. Brielle is alive, active, increasingly competent, and increasingly her own operator. The subject is adjusting to the parallel existence of a person whose welfare he cannot fully control and whose vocation he cannot fully prevent. The file expects this thread to be the dominant developmental axis of the next operational decade.

---

### Current Status: Operational, Geographic, Relational, Somatic

**Operational.** Active. Currently unaffiliated with any formal team. Maintains warm-but-distant contact with: Hannibal King (functional, the relationship having reached a stable plateau of mutual non-interference and occasional shared work); Doctor Voodoo / Jericho Drumm and the broader mystical defense cadre; Brielle Brooks and her circle, including her mother on a strictly cordial logistical basis; intermittent contact with surviving MI:13 alumni, including Faiza Hussain (now a senior figure in British supernatural medicine in her own right) and Spitfire. Estranged in the structural rather than acrimonious sense from most prior teammates; he does not return calls promptly but does return them.

**Geographic.** No fixed residence. The four inferred safe-houses remain active per behavioral pattern; the New Orleans property has, on the basis of recent appearances in Louisiana-set sequences, become the most-used. He is also observed transiting routinely through London (the Whitechapel basement remains), New York, and an as-yet unidentified location in the Carpathian foothills which the file suspects is a long-running anti-Dracula forward observation post.

**Relational.** The intimates list is small and stable: King, Faiza, Spitfire, Brielle, with secondary positions held by Drumm, Cage (residual from the Mighty Avengers period; cordial), and one or two others depending on operational era. He has not, on the documentary evidence, entered a new romantic partnership in the recent window. The Spitfire relationship persists in the unconsummated, mutually understood register it has occupied since MI:13 — neither party has acted to resolve it; both behave as if the resolution has already occurred and was a refusal. The file reads this as a stable accommodation rather than a frustration.

**Somatic.** Stable. Serum supply secured through multiple parallel sources, including post-Crane refined formulations that he is believed to be capable of synthesizing himself in a basic form. The Thirst is managed. No documented lapse in the recent window. Injury accumulation continues at the historical rate; healing factor unimpaired. He has been observed limping on two occasions in the past two operational years, both transient. The body remains the body it has been.

**Affective.** Constricted as ever, with the Brielle-axis exception. There is a marginal *softening* visible to the close reader — slightly more willingness to be drawn in panels in repose, slightly more dry humor in dialogue, slightly more tolerance for silence in the company of others. None of this is dramatic. All of it is real.

---

### How He Got Here: The Trajectory in Summary

The arc from MI:13 dissolution to the present is the arc of a man who:

1. **Lost a workplace** and discovered he had organized more of his identity around it than he had admitted;
2. **Drifted** through several operational years in a low-grade mourning he did not name;
3. **Experimented, briefly, with civic belonging** in a frame (Mighty Avengers) that recognized the racial and historical specificity of his existence, and discovered that integration was possible when the terms were correctly set;
4. **Was inducted, without seeking it, into the senior tier of mystical practice** by attrition and demonstrated competence, and accepted the role without enjoying it;
5. **Confronted the existence of a biological child** who inherits the wound and the gift in equal measure, and is presently reorganizing his entire sense of futurity around her existence;
6. **Continues to do the work**, at the same scale and quality he has done it for fifty operational years, while accumulating a fatigue that has no physiological correlate.

He is, at this moment, the most experienced operator in his specific field on the planet. He is unaccompanied. He is a father. He is doing what he has always done, with a single new fact — *she exists* — installed in the center of the operational picture. The file's assessment is that this fact is sufficient to bend the long-term trajectory, possibly for the first time since the alley in Soho. The direction of the bend is not yet legible. The bend itself is.

He will continue. He has no plan for after. He has, perhaps, the first plan he has ever had *for someone else's* after, and that is the development that the next phase of this file will track.


## Medical History

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## SECTION 6 — MEDICAL HISTORY

---

### 6.0 Framing Note

The subject's medical file is, in the strict sense, three files braided together: a human pediatric and adult chart that runs to roughly age nine and resumes only intermittently; a chimeric-physiology file that has no genuine precedent in clinical literature and must be reasoned analogically; and a forensic injury log of a kind ordinarily generated only by combatants in extended attritional warfare. Each must be treated on its own terms before they can be integrated. The integrating fact — present on every page — is that the subject's body is itself the contested ground of his life's question. He cannot relate to it neutrally. There is no "wellness check" register available to him; the body is either operational or compromised, and compromise is read morally before it is read clinically.

---

### 6.1 Perinatal Period: The Originating Event

The subject was delivered in obstructed labor at a Soho boarding house in late autumn. The attending physician was Deacon Frost, undiagnosed (and undiagnosable by the standards of the time) as a vampire. During the second stage of labor Frost fed on the parturient, Tara Brooks, producing exsanguination concurrent with delivery. The infant was extracted from a dying body and was transferred — through placental and direct mucosal contact with vampiric saliva at the moment of crowning — a load of Frost's enzymatic and viral material sufficient to alter ontogeny without producing conversion.

The clinical consequences of this single event are the architecture of every subsequent entry in this file:

- **Immunity to vampiric bite-conversion.** The standard vector of vampirism — saliva-borne — is ineffective in him. He has been bitten on multiple documented occasions across the canon (the Morbius incident notwithstanding, which proceeded by a different mechanism) without conversion.
- **Hemoglobin dependence.** A metabolic requirement for exogenous heme, manifesting clinically as the "Thirst." Onset latency from last dose is variable but in the operational record sits around 36–72 hours before prodromal symptoms and 5–10 days before functional decompensation.
- **Enhanced physical parameters.** Strength, speed, reflex latency, and sensory acuity scaled approximately 2–4× human baseline, with the upper end of that range available only in arousal states.
- **Accelerated tissue repair.** Closure of soft-tissue wounds in hours rather than days; bone remodeling in days rather than weeks; reconstitution of substantial blood loss within a sleep cycle given adequate caloric and heme intake.
- **Extended lifespan with arrested somatic aging.** Originally fixed in continuity as late-1920s birth, the subject presents phenotypically as a man in his mid-thirties across every published era. Telomeric or analogous arrest is presumed.
- **Diurnal tolerance.** The "daywalker" phenotype — full function under solar radiation, with mild photic discomfort under prolonged direct exposure reported only intermittently.

The psychological cargo of these facts is enormous and is treated section by section below. The umbrella fact is that the subject did not acquire his condition by choice or accident in adulthood but was born into it inside his mother's homicide. There is no pre-condition self to mourn. The grief, when it surfaces, is for a baseline he never had.

---

### 6.2 Childhood (Approx. Ages 0–9)

Records for this period are sparse and reconstructed from the subject's own later accounts to Afari, Harker, and (selectively) Hannibal King. Surrogate parenting by friends of the deceased mother in postwar London; nutrition adequate but not abundant; childhood illness profile presumed unremarkable, since none has ever been mentioned in canon and the dhampir immune profile would have suppressed the ordinary viral and bacterial roster. No record of vaccination. No record of dental care of any formal kind. The subject's adult dentition is intact, including the canines, which are slightly elongated but not overtly fanged — a somatic tell that he is photographically aware of and that explains the closed-mouth quality of his smile when one is permitted.

Two pediatric events of forensic interest. First, the recurrent dream of red eyes, beginning before language and reported intermittently across his life; this functions as the encoded memory of the perinatal event and is best classified as a pre-verbal traumatic intrusion rather than as a dream proper. Second, at approximately age nine, the alley intervention in which he killed his first vampire with a piece of broken wood while defending Jamal Afari. The medical residue of this event is minor — bruising, lacerations to the hands consistent with gripping splintered wood — but the neurological encoding is total. The kinesthetic memory of staking is, for him, the somatic substrate of belonging.

---

### 6.3 Adolescence and Apprenticeship (Approx. Ages 9–18)

Training under Afari produced the musculoskeletal profile he has carried since: dense lean mass, low body-fat percentage maintained without conscious dieting, exceptional grip strength, scapular and hip mobility consistent with decades of edged-weapons drilling. Repetitive-use signatures include slight asymmetric hypertrophy of the right forearm and shoulder, calluses across the metacarpophalangeal ridges of both hands, and a healed avulsion fracture pattern at the right ulnar styloid consistent with an early adolescent training injury that was not professionally set and remodeled on its own. He has full function but the joint sits perhaps two degrees off true; he favors it imperceptibly in fine motor work and compensates with the left when threading or fastening.

Childhood and adolescent scarring includes a curved line below the left jaw (a vampiric claw, age approximately twelve, by his own account to King), a series of short parallel marks across the lateral right thigh (training, blade-discipline drills with Afari), and a roughly circular cigarette burn on the inner left wrist whose provenance he has never disclosed and which is the only mark on him that does not have an offered story.

The Thirst was already manifest by mid-adolescence. Afari recognized it and managed it through whatever pre-serum improvisations were available — animal blood, primarily, supplemented by tightly rationed donations from sympathetic adults in their circle. The subject's lifelong revulsion at the act of feeding and his concurrent inability to stop needing to feed were laid down in this period. He associates the act with Afari's grave, patient, non-judgmental face, and the association is one of the few unambiguous tendernesses in his memory.

---

### 6.4 The Killing of Afari

When Afari was turned and the subject killed him, no physical injury of significance was recorded to the subject; he was at this point operationally proficient. The medical residue is entirely neuropsychiatric: the establishment of the recursive structure in which intimates become enemies, and the laying down of a procedural memory in which the act of killing a vampire is the act of preserving the loved object from what it has become. He does not, in any later combat, separate these two registers cleanly. Every staking is, at some level of processing, the staking of Afari and the rescue of him.

---

### 6.5 Adult Combat Injury Log (Selected and Categorized)

A complete enumeration would run to many hundreds of incidents. The taxonomy below captures the categories and their psychological residues.

**Penetrating thoracic trauma.** Documented impalements through the torso on at least four canonical occasions: through-and-through staking by Dracula-aligned hunters during the original Wolfman run; the chest wound from the early *Nightstalkers* arc; the abdominal impalement during the Frost-pursuit arcs of the late 1990s; and the spear wound during the MI:13 era (Dracula's lunar assault). Survival in each case attributable to dhampir healing; in each case the wound tracked near but did not perforate the heart, a fact he himself reads superstitiously, never aloud. The subject's chest and upper abdomen bear a cluster of healed entry-and-exit scars in the standard locations a vampire hunter would expect to find on himself, and he is reluctant to be seen shirtless even by intimates not because of the scars themselves but because they read, to him, as a topographical map of near-failures.

**Cervical injury.** At least one decapitation-adjacent neck wound (late Chichester era) requiring extended down-time for tracheal and vascular remodeling. Residual signature: a faint horizontal line across the anterior neck, visible only in raking light. Voice unchanged.

**Exsanguinating wounds.** Multiple. The interesting clinical detail is that he tolerates blood loss poorly relative to the rest of his durability — the same hemoglobin-dependent metabolism that requires exogenous heme appears to operate with little reserve, and a wound that a normal human might survive with transfusion produces in him a near-immediate Thirst spike. Combat tacticians who have worked with him (Wisdom, notably) have learned to keep serum within reach of his fallback positions.

**Burns.** Recurrent low-grade burns to the hands and forearms from sunlight-weapon backsplash (UV grenades, holy-water atomizers, silver-nitrate aerosols). He treats these casually; they heal within a sleep cycle. Two documented severe burn events — a Mephisto-aligned hellfire exposure during a Midnight Sons engagement, and a magical conflagration during the Spurrier-era *Death of Doctor Strange* sequence. Both produced visible scarring during the healing window and full resolution within days. The hellfire event left a persistent mild dysesthesia in the right palm that he has not mentioned to medical contacts.

**Blunt force trauma.** Continuous. Skull, ribs, long bones — virtually every survivable fracture pattern is in the subject's history. Notable: an old, badly remodeled fracture of the left fifth metacarpal (the boxer's fracture, from a fistfight in his pre-Afari years, by inference his only pre-vocation injury of note) which sits crooked and aches in cold weather, a fact he has admitted exactly once on the record (to King, in a Nightstalkers-era panel that the file flags as diagnostically rare).

**Magical and mystical wounds.** A different category clinically because they bypass the ordinary healing response. The Dormammu-aligned injury during a Strange Academy crossover required external occult intervention to close. The Chthonic wound during the Bryan Hill 2023–2024 run is, by the latest available data, *still partially open at the energetic level* and is the closest thing in his current file to a chronic condition with a defined locus. Subject manages it with disciplined wards and has refused offered healings on grounds that he is unwilling to incur the favor-debt.

**Bite wounds.** Numerous. The clinical curiosity is that they convert ordinary tissue damage into an additional metabolic insult — the saliva exposure, even without conversion, places a load on his system that he describes as nausea and that the file reads as a partial immune-recognition event analogous to a transfusion reaction. He showers immediately after such injuries when conditions allow. The compulsion to do so is forensic-grade.

---

### 6.6 The Morbius Conversion (Nightstalkers Era)

The full vampirization event under the Chichester run is the medical event of his life that he has most aggressively buried. Mechanism: bite by Michael Morbius under conditions that defeated the dhampir immune profile (the canonical explanation invokes the pseudo-vampiric nature of Morbius's biochemistry, which presented the antigen in a configuration his system was not pre-immunized against). Result: full vampiric phenotype for the duration of the arc — including hunger expression, predatory affect, photic vulnerability, and the loss of the daywalker tolerance.

Restoration was achieved through a combination of serum intervention and (per the run's own account) an act of will on the subject's part. The clinical residues are partial but durable:

- An olfactory and gustatory memory of having fed — not in dream but in body memory, the kind of memory that obtrudes when he passes the smell of fresh blood at a scene.
- A baseline-level reduction in his certainty about the firmness of the categorical line. Before Morbius he believed, structurally, that *he could not become it.* After Morbius he knows, structurally, that *he could.*
- A subtle change in operational style. Post-Morbius Blade is more procedurally cautious about his own behavioral monitoring. He has installed (and admitted to King) standing instructions that he be killed if he turns again and cannot be restored within a defined window.

The psychological cost is the largest single load on his current file. He does not speak about the Morbius arc. He will tolerate references to it only from King and (once) Faiza.

---

### 6.7 The Switchblade Dissociative Fugue

A months-long episode during the Chichester era in which the subject lived as an alternate-future assassin identity ("Switchblade") under supernatural and psychiatric stress combined. Clinically a dissociative fugue with co-occurring identity alteration, partially resolved on restoration but with persistent gaps in autobiographical recall for the period and persistent uncertainty about the moral content of acts committed during it. He has never sought clinical follow-up. His private resolution has been to assume the worst about what he did and to act, in the present, as if owing reparations to unnamed parties. This shows up operationally as a small, consistent pattern of pro bono interventions in cases where the obvious cost-benefit calculus would counsel disengagement.

The episode has not recurred in functional form. Subclinical micro-dissociations under extreme combat stress are reported by collaborators (Wisdom's MI:13 debriefs note "moments where he is somewhere else for a half-second") and are best read as ordinary combat dissociation rather than as a return of the fugue substrate.

---

### 6.8 The Thirst and the Serum: Pharmacological File

The central medical fact of his adult life. Source materials place the original serum under the development of Dr. Karl Crane and successor formulations under a rotating cast of biochemists (Strange's circles have contributed; Hank Pym is rumored in the file to have refined a batch). Current formulation: a hemoglobin-substitute analog with adjunctive enzymatic cofactors, administered orally on a roughly daily schedule with operational latitude of up to seventy-two hours under field conditions before prodromal symptoms.

**Withdrawal sequence (documented):**

- *Hours 24–48:* irritability, mild tremor in the dominant hand, hyperacuity of olfaction (he can smell blood at greater distance), narrowing of social tolerance.
- *Hours 48–96:* hyperalgesia, intrusive ideation regarding feeding, sleep disturbance, micro-tremor visible at rest, increase in the predatory cast of facial expression that collaborators report seeing without naming.
- *Days 5–10:* loss of fine motor regulation, impaired strategic judgment, increasing dominance of the predatory schema, eventual loss of impulse control and risk of unprovoked feeding.
- *Beyond day 10 (rarely observed in canon):* presumed full behavioral conversion in functional terms, even without physiological conversion.

**Behavioral scaffolding around the dependence:**

- Multiple geographically distributed serum caches, location-encoded such that no single compromise eliminates more than a fraction of supply.
- A daily dose ritual conducted in private, never observed even by intimates, treated with the formal seriousness of a religious observance.
- Standing arrangements with two named allies (King; in some eras, a second figure) to be sought out under specified shortage conditions, with pre-negotiated permissions for them to use force to restrain him.
- A revulsion-discipline around fresh human blood at scenes — he will not approach a bleeding civilian within an arm's length when he can avoid it.

**Psychological structure:** the dependence is, behaviorally, an opioid-maintenance topography. Rigid scheduling, hidden supply, supply-anxiety as a constant low-grade background, shame around any lapse, identity organized partly around competent management of the condition. He does not consider himself an addict in the moral sense; he considers himself a patient under permanent treatment. The distinction matters to him.

The Thirst is the only domain of his life in which he experiences *shame* as the primary affect rather than grief or rage. This is diagnostically central. Grief and rage have outward objects; shame turns inward and confirms the question he refuses to answer aloud.

---

### 6.9 Substances, Diet, Sleep, Maintenance

**Alcohol:** sparing. He will accept a drink in social-tactical settings and rarely finishes one. He does not trust the disinhibition.

**Tobacco:** none observed.

**Recreational substances:** none observed. The internal logic is consistent — any substance that alters his impulse-regulation interacts with the Thirst and is therefore categorically excluded.

**Caffeine:** moderate, instrumental. Coffee black, in operational settings.

**Diet:** high-protein, dense-calorie, eaten quickly and without ceremony when alone, with somewhat more attention when others are present (a social camouflage practice). He does not derive pleasure from food in any pattern the file can detect; eating is fueling.

**Sleep:** polyphasic by preference, monophasic when forced into civilian rhythms. Total sleep requirement estimated at 4–5 hours per 24, with brief restorative naps under operational load. He sleeps lightly, weapon within reach, in a configuration that places his body between any entry point and any other person in the room.

**Physical maintenance:** daily, non-negotiable. Edged-weapons drills, calisthenics, mobility work. Skipping a day is, by his own admission to King, a thing he has done perhaps three times in his adult life. Each was followed by visible somatic discomfort and rapid resumption.

**Dental and visual:** no professional care of either, ever. Both intact at chimeric baseline.

**Hygiene:** meticulous, with the post-bite shower compulsion noted above. Grooming minimalist but consistent — head shaved or close-cropped across most eras, beard maintained at constant length, fingernails trimmed shorter than fashion would dictate (a combat-residue habit).

---

### 6.10 Reproductive and Sexual Health

Limited documentation. The subject is, by report and observation, sexually functional but selectively active; partners across the canon are few and tend, as discussed elsewhere in this file, to be anomalous in ways that mirror his chimerism (Glory, Safron, Spitfire-adjacent material). Fertility status undetermined; no documented offspring in original continuity (the question is complicated by alternate-future material that lies outside the scope of this medical section). No documented sexually transmitted exposures; the dhampir immune profile is presumed to manage ordinary pathogen loads.

The psychological substrate of his sexual life is governed by the same attachment topology that governs his other intimacies. The body permits; the structure resists. He is not, by any available evidence, ascetic by ideology; he is constrained by the narrowness of the partner category he can tolerate.

---

### 6.11 Sensory Profile and Its Costs

Enhanced night vision to a degree that ordinary indoor lighting is mildly aversive; he prefers dim rooms and is photographically aware of which lights in any space he can dim or destroy unobtrusively. Olfactory acuity sufficient to identify vampires at distance by scent and to read emotional states of nearby humans by sweat composition — a capacity he does not advertise and that contributes to his apparent prescience in social encounters. Auditory acuity sufficient for sub-vocal detection at conversational range; he hears the heartbeats of those near him as a constant ambient layer.

The medical cost of these capacities is that *he cannot stand down.* The nervous system that in a normal human would constitute a panic-disordered hyperarousal state is his baseline, and is metabolically expensive. He compensates with the dense caloric and heme intake noted above. The phenomenological cost is that he has never experienced what a normal human would call a calm room. The closest approximation, by report, has been a small number of moments in the presence of Faiza Hussain, and these registered to him as anomalies requiring explanation rather than as states to be sought.

---

### 6.12 Aging, Lifespan, and the Question of Endpoint

He is chronologically near a century old in original continuity and presents as a man in his mid-thirties. The endpoint of his life is undetermined by ordinary actuarial reasoning. He has, by the file's read, never seriously planned for an old age, because he does not anticipate one — not from despair but from a structural assumption that the work will end him before time does. This is not stated; it is inferred from the absence of any retirement infrastructure (no property accumulation, no pension equivalents, no investment in skills that have no operational use) and from the consistent pattern of leaving relationships before they can mature into something requiring a future.

The file's clinical judgment is that the absence of an old-age plan is itself a medical-psychological datum and belongs in this section rather than in the personality section, because it shapes daily behavior in ways the subject does not articulate. He uses his body as if it were borrowed; he does not save it.

---

### 6.13 Integrating Summary

The medical history is, taken together, the somatic register of the same fact that organizes every other section of this file: the subject was constituted by an event he cannot remember in a body he did not choose, and has built a life that consists of the disciplined management of that body in the service of preventing the event's recurrence in others. The injuries are the receipts of that life. The dependence is its daily liturgy. The scars are its archive. There is no body separate from the work, and the work has, in its turn, become the only relationship to the body he can sustain.

He will continue this until the body fails or the work does. Neither, by the present evidence, is imminent. Both, by the present evidence, are inevitable. The file notes — without recommendation — that no clinician has ever been permitted full access to him, and that the closest thing to a physician in his life is a vampire who refuses to feed.


## Somatic Atlas

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## Section VI — SOMATIC ATLAS

---

The body is the primary document. The subject has spent roughly a century inside it, training it, wounding it, and listening to it, and what reads to civilians as taciturnity is in fact the silence of a man whose somatic feedback is louder than most ambient speech. What follows is the granular record — every observable sign that a competent surveillance file would catalogue across a year of continuous coverage, cross-indexed by behavioral state.

---

### 1. Architecture and Carriage

**Build.** Mesomorphic, dense rather than bulky; the musculature reads as functional rather than displayed. Lat development pronounced (legacy of edged-weapon work, climbing, the falling-and-catching mechanics of nest-clearing); deltoid-trapezius shelf heavily developed from decades of overhand striking and throwing-blade work; forearms disproportionate to upper arm, with the flexor mass on the dominant (right) side measurably greater. Hip-to-shoulder ratio narrow; the body is built to pivot. Resting body fat estimated low single digits — not from cosmetic discipline but from the metabolic cost of the chimerism and the serum regimen.

**Resting posture (calm/operational baseline).** Weight distributed 60/40 onto the rear foot in standing; never fully square. When seated, the chair is angled obliquely to the room, never with back to door; he selects the position before he is conscious of selecting it, and a surveillance operator watching him enter a café over fifty consecutive visits will record the same chair-rotation roughly 49 times. Hands at rest fall to the thighs, palms down, fingers slightly spread — not folded, not pocketed; pocketed hands are slow hands. Shoulders carried low and back but not military-rigid; the chest is open without being displayed.

**Posture under stress.** Almost no visible change. The signature is *what stops* rather than what starts: the small idle micro-movements (the slow rotation of a ring he does not wear, a residual habit-loop; the occasional toe-flex inside the boot) cease. He becomes more still, and the stillness is the tell. Trained observers — Wisdom, Strange, King — read the cessation as a klaxon.

**Posture under threat.** The center of mass drops one to three centimeters; the rear knee unlocks; the hands re-zero from thighs to the dead space at the hip-line where the blade lives. He does not crouch — the silhouette stays largely unchanged to an untrained witness — but the loading is total. He can move from this posture into a full committed strike in under 200 milliseconds; the loading itself is the strike, only deferred.

**Posture in intimacy.** The least studied state and the most diagnostic. The shoulders carry *higher* than baseline (he does not relax them — relaxation is unfamiliar enough to register as a threat-cue to his own nervous system); the chin drops minutely; he positions himself so that the intimate is in his peripheral rather than central field, which reads to the intimate as inattention and is, in fact, the highest available trust signal — he has placed them in the zone reserved for allies, not targets. With Faiza Hussain across the MI:13 run, observers can see this repeatedly: he stands with her at his four-o'clock, not in front of him.

---

### 2. Gait and Locomotion

**Walk.** Heel-strike soft, almost a roll onto the midfoot; cadence approximately 105–110 steps per minute at ambient speed, slightly slower than the average urban male, because he is reading the street as he crosses it. Step length even. Arm swing minimal — the dominant arm swings perhaps two-thirds of the natural amplitude, the off arm slightly more. The asymmetry preserves the draw line on the right side.

**Tactical movement.** When operational, the heel-strike disappears entirely; he moves forefoot-first, knees soft, weight kept directly over the supporting foot to allow instantaneous direction change. He can cross a hardwood floor in low light without producing a measurable acoustic signature; this is not stealth as art but stealth as decades of habituation. He does not "sneak" — he simply walks as he walks, and the walk happens to be silent.

**Stairs.** Ascends on the balls of the feet, two at a time when alone, one at a time when accompanied (he matches civilian rhythm to remain unremarkable). Descends with the off hand brushing the wall, not the rail; the rail is what an off-balance assailant grabs. He has never, in any recorded appearance, descended a stairwell facing forward when the building is unknown to him — he sidesteps, leading with the off shoulder.

**Doorways.** Pauses at threshold for between 200 and 600 milliseconds. To civilians this looks like hesitation or politeness; it is the olfactory and acoustic sweep that his sensorium runs involuntarily. He enters with the dominant hand trailing, body angled, never fully presenting the centerline. He clears corners with the eyes before the feet.

**Vehicles.** Sits behind the driver when chauffeured, behind the passenger seat when driving cover for someone else. Drives himself in older manual-transmission machines — the canon has put him in muscle cars and motorcycles across eras — because the clutch foot is a body-cue he uses to stay engaged. He does not use cruise control. Mirrors checked at a rate noticeably above civilian baseline; a metronomic three-second sweep.

---

### 3. Hands

The hands are the most informative single region of the body. They are large, scarred across the dorsa with old defensive cuts (the typical pattern of someone who has caught blades on the back of the forearm and hand for decades), with knuckles thickened from striking work but not the gnarled, broken-and-reset look of an unschooled brawler — his striking surfaces have been conditioned, not abused. Nails kept very short, square-cut; he files rather than clips, because clipping leaves edges and edges catch on clothing during a draw. The right thumb pad shows a slight callus from blade-grip indexing.

**At rest.** Open, palms down on thigh or table. He does not steeple. He does not pocket. Fingers never interlaced — interlaced fingers take time to free.

**Talking.** Minimal hand gesture; what gesture exists is small and contained within the lap-to-chest envelope. He does not point with the index finger; when he must indicate something he uses an open hand, palm up, fingers loose — a gesture inherited from teaching and from never wanting to look like he is drawing.

**Stressed.** A specific tell: the right thumb rubs once, slowly, across the pads of the right index and middle fingers, as if testing for blood or grit. Repeats at irregular intervals. Almost no other hand-movement intrudes. The thumb-rub is the only somatic leak the trained eye can rely on, and it is itself so subtle that civilians miss it across hours of contact.

**Threat.** Hands move to the dead-hang position at the hip line and *stay there* — they do not visibly load the blade until commitment. The off hand floats forward perhaps ten centimeters, palm angled in toward the centerline, ready to parry or grip. The fingers extend rather than curl; relaxed digits move faster than tensed ones.

**Intimacy.** Hands become uncharacteristically slow and deliberate. Touch is initiated by him only rarely and is preceded by a perceptible pause — the moment in which he is overriding the body's default refusal. When he does touch, the contact is firmer than expected (he has miscalibrated for normal-human fragility his entire life and is only intermittently corrected by the partner) and is most often placed at the shoulder, the upper arm, or the back of the neck — never the face. The face is reserved.

---

### 4. Face

A face built for not being read. Long-jawed, high cheekbones, brow ridge that shadows the eyes in most lighting — anatomy that does most of the work the affect-flattening does in conversation.

**Eyes.** Dark; pupils visibly responsive in low light at a speed that would alarm an ophthalmologist briefed honestly. Saccade pattern under observation is the diagnostic feature: in any room he has not previously cleared, his gaze runs a fixed sweep — entries, exits, elevated lines, the hands of every person present, the reflective surfaces, the floor for blood-trace or salt-line — in roughly four seconds, then settles. The settled gaze appears restful and is not; it is a held framing within which peripheral motion is continuously parsed. He maintains direct gaze in conversation longer than is comfortable, which civilians read as intensity or hostility and which is, structurally, his refusal to break the predator's eye-contact discipline even in social registers.

**Mouth.** Default position closed, lips relaxed, very slight downturn at the corners — not a frown, an absence of smile-tonus. He smiles rarely; when he does, in the early Wolfman era the smile was wide and quick and weaponized (the quip-delivery), in the modern register the smile is a single asymmetric lift at the right corner, gone in under a second. The asymmetric lift is the closest thing he produces to laughter in public.

**Jaw.** A masseter habit: under stress, a single slow clench-and-release on the left side, visible as a flicker beneath the cheek. Under sustained stress, the clench-release establishes a slow rhythm at perhaps one cycle per three to four seconds. This is the most reliable somatic stress index after the thumb-rub.

**Brow.** Almost never lifted. The brow stays low and level; surprise is registered by a brief widening of the eyes alone. Concentration produces a slight medial knit, no more than a millimeter or two of skin gather.

**Micro-expressions.** Catalogued across the canon: a flash of disgust (upper lip lift, nostril flare) on the recognition of vampiric scent in a crowd, usually suppressed within 100 milliseconds; a flash of grief (inner brow lift, slight eye-closure) on any unguarded reference to Tara Brooks or Afari, suppressed within 200 milliseconds; a flash of contempt (unilateral lip corner pull) toward incompetent authority, frequently *not* suppressed.

**Eyewear.** Sunglasses worn far more often than required. The functional rationale (light sensitivity at the high end of his sensorium) is real; the operational rationale (denying observers the saccade-read) is the actual one. The frames are dark, wraparound or aviator-cut depending on era, replaced often — he treats them as consumable.

---

### 5. Voice

Baritone, dry-toned, resonant in the chest rather than the head. Volume kept consistently below ambient — interlocutors lean in, which both flatters and tactically commits them. Cadence slow, with pauses placed where civilians would place filler. He does not use *uh* or *um*. Sentences end on a slight downward inflection, even questions; the upward question-inflection is reserved for moments when he is deliberately performing approachability.

Accent is an American-inflected English with residual London substrate audible on certain vowels (the *a* in *can't*, the *o* in *don't*) — a hybrid that no native of either place would place correctly, which is operationally useful.

**Under stress.** Volume drops further, not rises. Pace slows. The voice acquires a granular roughness in the lower register. Anyone who has worked with him learns that the quieter he becomes the closer the violence is.

**With intimates.** A measurable softening of the consonant edges; the *t* and *d* stops become less percussive. He uses fewer words. The silences lengthen and are no longer tactical.

**With Frost-coded stimuli.** The cadence breaks. Sentences shorten to clauses; the granular roughness rises into the mid-register; volume occasionally fails him in the other direction and a single word will come out louder than intended. This is the only context in which his voice misbehaves.

---

### 6. Grooming and Self-Maintenance

The grooming regime is monastic and consistent across decades. Head shaved or kept to a millimeters-short fade — he maintains it himself with a straight razor and a hand mirror, sitting, never standing, never in a public barber's chair. The goatee is kept tight, edges precise; he trims it every second or third day on a fixed schedule. Hands and nails maintained as above. Skin care minimal but disciplined — he washes with unscented soap (scent is a tracking liability and an olfactory irritant to his own nose).

**Wardrobe.** Functional, dark, layered. The outer garment is always something that breaks silhouette and conceals the blade — leather coat in earlier eras, technical shells in modern depictions. Trousers tactical-cut with reinforced knees and inseam, allowing full hip articulation; boots ankle-height, soft-soled, with the laces double-knotted and the bow tucked. He owns very few items; what he owns is identical or near-identical across copies. The wardrobe is a uniform.

**Smell.** Notable absence of cologne or aftershave. His own scent — to those whose sensoria can read it — carries the faint metallic-pharmaceutical signature of the serum.

**Hygiene under field conditions.** Maintains shaving and grooming even in extended operations; will sterilize wounds before sleeping. Refuses to operate dirty; the discipline is partly tactical (infection in his system has unpredictable interactions with the chimerism) and partly psychological — a degraded body is a degraded line between him and what he hunts.

---

### 7. Sleep Architecture

Sleeps in two segments rather than one — a long block of three to four hours in the late morning (his diurnal cycle is shifted; he is functionally crepuscular-to-nocturnal) and a shorter block of ninety minutes to two hours in the late afternoon. Total sleep need approximately five to six hours per twenty-four, reduced from human baseline by the chimerism. Sleeps in a recoverable position — on the back or the side facing the door, never prone, never facing the wall.

**Pre-sleep ritual.** Weapons checked and placed within arm's reach in a specific order (primary blade, secondary blade, sidearm if carried, serum injector). The room's exits noted. The door barricaded or trapped per circumstance. Boots placed at the bedside with laces loosened to the exact tension that allows one-motion donning.

**Sleep onset.** Fast — under ten minutes — and this is its own discipline. He has trained the parasympathetic transition the way other men train the draw.

**Sleep architecture proper.** REM-heavy. The dreams, on the rare occasions they have been depicted in canon, are dominated by two recurring contents: the mother (an image he has constructed, since he has no memory of her) and the alley with Afari. Wakes from these without verbal sound — a sharp inhalation, eyes open, hand on the blade before consciousness is fully restored. The hand-on-blade-before-consciousness is the single most reliable sleep-cycle behavior in the file.

**Sleep with another person present.** Rare and revealing. He sleeps lighter, wakes more often, but specifically positions himself between the intimate and the door. The protective placement is unconscious and consistent.

---

### 8. Feeding and the Serum

The somatic centerpiece. He eats sparingly and on schedule rather than appetite; the serum suppresses appetite while meeting metabolic load. Real-food intake skews to high-protein and iron-dense (rare beef, organ meats when available) — the body is asking, and he answers it as far as he can within the line he has drawn.

**The serum administration itself.** Performed in private without exception. The site rotates between the antecubital fossae and the lateral thigh on a tracked schedule to prevent tissue damage. The injection is preceded by a perceptible pause — a held breath, eyes closed for two to three seconds — that is not present in any other procedural act he performs. He does not look at the needle going in. He looks at the needle coming out, to confirm. After dosing he washes his hands, even when they are already clean.

**Behavior approaching dose-time.** A subtle increase in the masseter clench-rhythm. The thumb-rub frequency rises. A specific tongue-against-the-canine micro-movement appears — the canines themselves are normal human anatomy, but the tongue knows the geometry the body believes it should have. Mood compresses further. He becomes more economical with words.

**Behavior in early Thirst (missed dose, four to eight hours overdue).** Hyperacusis becomes overt — he flinches at sounds he would ordinarily filter. The hand tremor is fine and confined to the off hand. Sweat appears at the hairline and the small of the back. He withdraws from company.

**Behavior in established Thirst (twelve-plus hours).** Pupils dilated beyond ambient justification. Speech reduced to monosyllables or refused. The olfactory tracking becomes involuntary and visible — head turns toward unseen blood-sources. He will physically remove himself from civilians at this point and has, across canon, locked himself in vehicles, basements, and on one occasion a meat locker, to manage it.

**Shame response.** The only state in which he avoids eye contact. After a near-lapse or a managed-crisis Thirst event, he is silent for hours and will not be in the same room as anyone who witnessed it for as long as he can manage. The shame is the only affect he cannot metabolize through the usual sublimation; it sits in the body as a kind of postural collapse — the shoulders, for once, drop.

---

### 9. Sexual and Affectional Behavior

The most under-documented domain and the one where the surveillance file must work hardest from inference. The canon depicts him as having had a small number of lovers across a long life; the through-line is that each was either supernatural, supernatural-adjacent, or operationally embedded in his world. Civilian partners do not appear.

Initiation is rarely his; he is responsive rather than pursuing. The somatic register in early intimacy is the *higher-shoulder, slowed-hand* pattern noted above — the body treats the encounter as a controlled exposure to a feared category. Touch reciprocated is slower and firmer than received. He does not vocalize. He does not speak during sex except in response to direct address.

Post-coital pattern: he does not sleep in the bed. He sits, or stands at the window, or leaves entirely. This is sometimes read by partners as rejection and is, in his internal frame, the most basic perimeter discipline — someone has been allowed close enough to alter his sensorium, and the perimeter must be re-established. With longer-tenured partners he has learned, partially, to remain.

Affection in non-sexual registers is delivered through proximity and protection rather than verbal or facial channels. He stands closer to those he cares about than to others. He positions himself between them and entrances. He is, with Faiza specifically across the MI:13 run, observed to angle his body so that any incoming hostile would have to cross him to reach her, and to do this without apparent awareness that he is doing it.

---

### 10. Tics, Idiosyncrasies, Residuals

**The thumb-rub.** The signature tell.

**The masseter clench.** Stress index.

**The tongue-to-canine.** Pre-dose signal.

**The doorway pause.** Sensory sweep, mistaken for hesitation.

**The chair rotation.** Geometry preference, invariant.

**The ring that isn't there.** Right ring finger occasionally rotated by the thumb as if a band were present; no band has ever been depicted. The residual likely indexes an object — a memento, a weapon-grip — that the body learned and the conscious mind has forgotten.

**The single fingertip rest against the carotid.** Performed on himself two to four times daily, ostensibly checking pulse; functionally a self-soothing contact and a serum-effect monitor.

**The acoustic re-cue.** When startled by an unidentified sound, he turns the head a precise fifteen to twenty degrees off-axis, presenting the better ear and clearing the line of sight in the same motion. Universal across eras.

**The grief-swallow.** On the rare occasions the mother or Afari is invoked, a single visible swallow precedes any verbal response, regardless of what the response is. He has not, across fifty years of recorded contact, found a way to suppress this one.

**The non-laugh.** A short single exhalation through the nose, mouth closed, in response to something he finds genuinely amusing. He does not produce laughter sound. Civilians often miss it; intimates learn to register it as the warmest signal he emits.

---

### 11. State-Shift Summary Table (Prose)

In the **calm operational baseline** that constitutes perhaps 85% of his waking life, the body presents as controlled, economical, slightly under-active, with the perimeter disciplines (chair, doorway, sweep, mirror-rhythm) running unconsciously and the leak-tells (thumb-rub, masseter, tongue-canine) at low frequency.

Under **acute stress** the body grows more still rather than more active; the leak-tells rise in frequency; voice drops; saccade rate increases beneath the sunglasses; the hands re-zero to the hip-line.

Under **threat** the center of mass drops, the rear knee unlocks, hands load to dead-hang, the face flattens further, and the breath cycle lengthens — he breathes more slowly under threat than under stress, an inverted profile from the civilian norm.

In **intimacy** the shoulders ride higher, the hands slow, touch is delivered firmer than received, the voice softens at the consonants, and the perimeter discipline does not disengage — it is repurposed around the intimate as protected object.

In **dose-due or Thirst onset** the masseter rhythm rises, the tongue-canine appears, the hand tremors fine on the off side, the olfactory tracking becomes involuntary, and he withdraws physically; in established Thirst the pupils dilate, speech fails, and he self-isolates.

In **Frost-adjacent activation** the voice misbehaves, the cadence breaks, tactical discipline degrades in the specific vector of *over-commitment toward the target*, and the grief-swallow appears even without verbal cue.

In **shame** — post-Thirst, post-lapse — the shoulders finally drop, eye contact is lost, and the silence is absolute. This is the only state in which the body, briefly, lets go of itself.

---

*End Section VI. See Section VII (Routines, Rituals, and Spatial Patterns) for the temporal scaffolding within which these somatic patterns are organized.*


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## Section 6 — Attachment & Relational Patterns

---

### 6.1 Origin of the Attachment Substrate

The attachment system of any human being is laid down across the first thirty-six months of postnatal life through repeated, predictable, regulated interaction with a primary caregiver whose body and face the infant uses as a tuning fork. The subject's case is unusual in that the foundational layer of this process was not merely disrupted — disruption is common and survivable — but *coincident with the inciting violence of his entire adult vocation*. Tara Brooks did not die at six months postpartum, leaving an infant with eighteen weeks of regulated co-presence to draw on; she did not die in childbirth from natural causes, leaving the child with a mournable absence framed by impersonal biology. She was fed upon, by a physician she had trusted, while delivering. The infant's first sensory data — the only data the limbic apparatus had to organize itself around — was almost certainly the maternal cortisol cascade of being killed, the smell and sound of arterial loss at proximity, and the absence of regulatory response from the body he was emerging from.

He cannot consciously recall any of this. The somatic memory system, which encodes pre-verbal experience without narrative tagging, has retained the entire event as procedural priming. This is the substrate. Everything in the file builds on it.

The subsequent caregiving picture compounds rather than repairs. Soho boarding-house women — the friends of Tara Brooks who took the infant in — provided physical care without the consistency of a single attuned figure. He was passed among households, fed and changed but not *minded* in the technical sense. The earliest stable narrative he was offered about his own origin was that "a man with red eyes" killed his mother — a story given to a four- or five-year-old by adults who had no better explanation and who, in offering it, inadvertently installed in him the cognition that *the world contains a hidden predator class and you are uniquely positioned to recognize it.* This was, before any conscious decision, his identity.

Jamal Afari, the elderly jazz trumpeter, enters at approximately age nine. The alley intervention is the central scene of his life and is decisive for attachment in a way that has not been adequately mapped in prior assessments. What occurred in functional terms: a child, alone and unbonded, encountered an adult under lethal threat, took action that saved the adult, and was *taken in as a consequence of the violence he committed.* This is the conditioning trial that fixes every subsequent relational pattern. The lesson the nervous system extracted — and it was extracted in a single trial, because high-arousal learning consolidates without rehearsal — is **I am permitted to have a person if I am useful against the predators. The price of belonging is performance.**

Afari then trained him for roughly a decade in the disciplines that would let him repeat the performance reliably. Edged weapons, ranged stakes, folklore-mechanics. Affection between them was real and is depicted as such in the *Tomb of Dracula* flashbacks, but it was always braided with the vocation. There was no parallel domain — no Saturday-morning interval, no birthdays unconnected to operational milestones — in which the boy was loved *off-duty*. When Afari was turned and Eric killed him, the conditioning was completed by the negative side of the contingency: *the person I belong to will become what I hunt, and I will have to perform the act on him.* The recursion was sealed.

### 6.2 Operational Attachment Style

The convergent diagnostic read is **disorganized attachment with a dismissive-avoidant operational overlay.** The disorganized substrate (Main & Solomon's Type D) is visible whenever the attachment system is activated under stress — he displays the classic signature of approach-avoidance oscillation around figures who could matter to him, freezing-and-pivoting at moments of incipient closeness, and a tendency to introduce hostile or self-sabotaging behavior precisely at the threshold of intimacy. The dismissive overlay (Bartholomew's Type 3) is the social presentation he has built across decades to make the disorganized substrate manageable in field conditions: terse, self-sufficient, affect-flattened, framing relational needs as operational liabilities.

The two layers are observably non-fused. Under ordinary conditions the dismissive overlay holds and he presents as a high-functioning lone operator. Under conditions that activate the substrate — Frost-coded stimuli, threats to his narrow intimates, prolonged forced proximity with a person who refuses to be repelled by his perimeter (Faiza Hussain is the textbook case) — the disorganized layer leaks: micro-approach behaviors followed by sudden withdrawal, statements of care immediately retracted into procedural framings, an inability to accept a gesture of warmth that is reciprocated rather than transactional.

### 6.3 The Bonding Sequence — What It Looks Like From First Contact

The pattern is regular enough across fifty years of canon to be diagrammed.

**Phase 1 — Predator Screen (seconds to minutes).** Every new figure is processed through the involuntary olfactory and behavioral assessment that his sensorium runs continuously. *Is this a vampire. Is this a thrall. Is this a civilian. Is this a competent operator. Is this a liability.* The taxonomy is sharp and exclusive; there is no provisional category. The screen is not paranoid in the clinical sense — it is veridical, given his world — but it has the structural effect of paranoia: every interaction begins with classification rather than greeting.

**Phase 2 — Tactical Bracketing (first encounter to first shared operation).** Having classified, he assigns the figure a tactical role and behaves toward them entirely within it. With operators: clipped coordination, dry humor, no biographical disclosure. With civilians: protective distance, minimal verbal engagement, an instruction or two and then absence. With potential allies: a probing test, often disguised as procedural friction, designed to elicit either competence or withdrawal. He has been observed across multiple runs deliberately under-explaining a tactical situation to a new ally to see whether they ask the right question; those who do are upgraded, those who do not are written off.

**Phase 3 — Reluctant Provisional Trust (months).** If the figure survives Phase 2 and continues to demonstrate either competence (operators) or stubborn presence (intimates), he extends a narrow provisional trust. The form is operational reliance — he will take their cover, he will share a vehicle, he will accept a wound dressing — without parallel disclosure. He still tells them nothing about himself that is not already in the public file. Quincy Harker, who worked alongside him for years in the Wolfman run, received almost no autobiographical disclosure until very late; the same pattern is documented with Pete Wisdom in MI:13.

**Phase 4 — The Single Disclosure (rare, often non-verbal).** At some inflection point, usually following a near-loss of the figure or of himself, he makes one disclosure. It is almost always a single sentence, delivered flatly, often about his mother or about Afari. It is the signal that the figure has crossed into the small set of those he has admitted are real to him. He does not repeat it; he does not elaborate when asked; he treats subsequent inquiries as if the disclosure had not occurred. The disclosure is the bond, not the beginning of an ongoing process of relational deepening.

**Phase 5 — Steady-State Tolerated Intimacy.** Once a figure is inside, the relationship stabilizes at a low-bandwidth, high-reliability mode. He will appear for them. He will accept calls he would not accept from anyone else. He will return to a location for them that he would otherwise leave. He still does not initiate emotional content, still does not seek them out when not operationally required, still cannot tolerate sustained civilian proximity. The intimacy is real and the bandwidth is fixed; he cannot push it higher even when the figure invites him to.

**Phase 6 — The Departure.** Across virtually every long-running affiliation in canon — the Harker cell, the Nightstalkers, MI:13, the Mighty Avengers, the Midnight Sons — the same termination pattern obtains. Without a precipitating betrayal, often without a precipitating event at all, he leaves. The leaving is rarely framed in language; he is, on a given morning, no longer there. He maintains thread contact — he will return if called for a genuine operation — but the steady-state presence is withdrawn before it can be taken from him by the relational mechanism he expects: someone becoming what he hunts.

### 6.4 Distrust — Its Mechanics and Its Limits

Distrust in the subject is not the suspicious affect of the chronically wronged. It is a default analytical posture, calibrated rather than emotional, that costs him almost nothing to maintain and which he relinquishes only on evidence. He does not distrust *people* — he distrusts *categories*, and assigns persons to categories on observation.

The categories that receive structural distrust: vampires (with the King and Spitfire exceptions, both managed by a permanent watchfulness he himself acknowledges); telepaths and reality-warpers (because the *mother-illusion vector* is the canonical lever against him and he knows it); institutional authorities offering protection (because his earliest model of authority was a physician who fed on his mother — the file shows a documented allergic response to medical settings and to figures presenting as healers, with Faiza the lone overcome exception); and figures who attempt rapid intimacy (he reads accelerated approach as either operational deception or as the kind of need he cannot meet).

The limits of his distrust are diagnostic. Once a figure has cleared the bonding sequence, distrust toward *them* essentially zeroes out, even when ordinary prudence would maintain a reserve. He is, with his small set of intimates, structurally under-defended — Hannibal King has come within hours of full vampiric relapse multiple times and Blade has not adjusted the relationship; Spitfire's partial vampirism does not generate the suspicion it would in any other case. This is the dismissive overlay reversing: having organized the world into trusted and untrusted, he cannot grade the trusted category, only expel from it. This makes him manipulable along precisely one axis: an established intimate compromised against their will.

### 6.5 Betrayal — Its Forms and His Response

The canon documents three structurally distinct betrayal experiences, and his response to each is informative.

**Betrayal by conversion** (Afari, multiple lovers across the runs, near-misses with King). The intimate is not turned against him by choice; they are turned into the predator class by infection. His response is grief metabolized as duty: he kills the converted figure, often himself, and registers the loss in the somatic discharge channels (extended training, increased operational tempo, longer solo intervals) rather than in language. He does not blame the converted figure. He does not appear to revise the relationship retrospectively. The grief sits where it sits and the operational pattern continues.

**Betrayal by choice** (the various human-faction adversaries who have used him; some of the institutional manipulations in the *Nightstalkers* and MAX-era runs). The response is colder and more durable. He does not seek revenge in the operatic sense; he simply removes the figure from any future cooperative frame and, if they are an operational threat, neutralizes them with the same methodology he uses for vampires. There is no documented case of a human betrayer being readmitted to his trust.

**Betrayal by his own physiology** (the Morbius conversion; the Switchblade dissociation; near-Thirst lapses). This is the betrayal he metabolizes worst. It is the only domain in which the canon documents shame as opposed to grief or rage. The post-conversion period after the Morbius incident is depicted with a withdrawal and self-monitoring intensity that exceeds his response to any external betrayal. The structural reason is clear: external betrayals confirm his existing model of the world; internal betrayals threaten the line — *I am not that* — on which his entire personality is built.

### 6.6 Repair — What It Requires and Why It Almost Never Happens

The subject has limited repair capacity in the conventional relational sense because the operations of repair require sustained verbal engagement with relational content, and that engagement is, for him, physiologically and characterologically intolerable. He cannot sit across from an intimate and process a rupture in language for forty minutes. He can sit across from an intimate in silence for forty minutes, having returned to them after the rupture, and let the proximity itself constitute the repair.

This is not absence of repair; it is non-verbal repair, operating on the same channel as the original bonding (presence, mutual operational risk, tolerated proximity). It works only with figures who can read it. Faiza Hussain demonstrably can. Hannibal King demonstrably can — he and the subject have repaired multiple ruptures across their decades-long association without, so far as the canon records, ever discussing one. With figures who require verbal repair, ruptures are typically terminal: the subject does not have the language and will not perform an emotional register he does not feel, so the relationship ends by his withdrawal rather than by acknowledged break.

A documented sub-pattern: when he *has* attempted verbal repair, it has taken the form of a single sentence offered out of context, often weeks after the rupture, often about something tangential, which the addressee is expected to decode as the apology it is. Those who decode it remain in the trusted set; those who require him to be explicit do not.

### 6.7 Intimacy and Dependency

The intimacy pattern resolves into two operating principles, both of which derive from the substrate.

**First principle: intimacy is permitted only with anomalies.** This has been noted in the shared assessment and is worth granular elaboration. The canonical intimates — Hannibal King, Faiza Hussain, Spitfire, and in lesser registers various Nightstalkers and the Harker line — each occupy a structural position that mirrors or complements his own chimerism. King is a vampire who refuses predation: the proof that the category is not destiny. Spitfire is a partial vampire with a heroic identity intact: the bridge image that legitimizes his own composition. Faiza is a doctor of devout faith and irrepressible warmth: the inverse of the physician-predator who killed his mother and the structural repair-figure for that originating wound. The pattern is so consistent that it constitutes a selection rule rather than a preference. Ordinary humans cannot be admitted because they cannot survive his world and because their ordinariness implicitly accuses him of his own composition; ordinary vampires cannot be admitted because they are the enemy. He bonds at the boundaries, with figures who themselves live on the line he lives on.

**Second principle: dependency is asymmetric and unidirectional.** He permits intimates to depend on him — he is, in operational terms, a remarkably reliable protective figure once a person is inside the set — but he does not permit himself to depend on them in any register he can name. He will accept tactical assistance, will accept medical care from Faiza, will accept King's flanking in a fight, but he will not request emotional support and will not acknowledge having received it. The asymmetry is not vanity or pride; it is the structural impossibility of admitting a need that, if denied or withdrawn, would re-enact the original loss. He keeps the dependency channel closed because he cannot tolerate its potential interruption. The intimates who endure are those who provide support without naming it, who let him receive without acknowledgment, and who do not require the closing of the loop.

A sub-pattern observable across the romantic-adjacent relationships in canon: he will accept physical intimacy more easily than emotional intimacy, but in both cases he tends to terminate the relationship — through his own withdrawal or through tolerating its dissolution — before it reaches the point at which his daily life would have to reorganize around the other person. He has never, in fifty years of published material, lived with a partner in any sustained civilian sense. The closest approximation is the operational cohabitation of the Nightstalkers, which is closer to a military barracks than to a household.

### 6.8 The Relational Template — The Pattern That Repeats

The template, in its fully articulated form, runs as follows. It can be observed in the Afari trajectory, in the Harker relationship, in the Quincy-then-Edith Harker generational continuity, in the King partnership, in the Faiza bond, in the Spitfire adjacency, in the various Nightstalkers, in Pete Wisdom, in the recent Bryan Hill–era relationships, and in his complicated near-bonds with figures like Strange and Wong. It is the single template he runs.

1. **Encounter under operational duress.** The relationship begins in a situation of mutual lethal threat or shared mission. He has almost no relationships that began in civilian space; those that did were rapidly converted to operational frames before he could engage with them.

2. **Demonstration of competence or stubbornness.** The other party either proves operationally useful or refuses to be repelled by his perimeter. This is the gate.

3. **Provisional reliance, no disclosure.** He works alongside them, accepts their cover, gives them his back in fights, while telling them nothing.

4. **A near-loss event.** Either he nearly loses them or they nearly lose him. The event activates the substrate.

5. **Single disclosure or single non-verbal gesture.** The bond is sealed by one act that the addressee must read correctly. If they do, the relationship becomes structural.

6. **Steady-state low-bandwidth intimacy.** He is reliably present in narrow operational and protective ways and absent in the wide registers of ordinary closeness.

7. **A test he himself introduces.** At some point, often months or years in, he behaves in a way calculated — not consciously, but reliably — to test whether the figure will reject him. Rude departures, refusals to attend, a stretch of unanswered communication. The figures who pass this test remain.

8. **An eventual rupture or departure.** Either the relationship terminates because the figure becomes what he hunts (conversion, corruption, death from supernatural cause), or he himself withdraws before that can happen. The departure is rarely framed in language. The thread is left open for operational re-contact.

9. **Memorialization through vocation.** The lost figure is integrated into the ongoing vocation as a private referent — Afari is invoked in his training methodology, Tara is invoked in every Frost engagement, lost lovers and partners are invoked in target selection. He does not grieve in language; he grieves in *aim*.

The template is the personality. Every relationship he has ever had, with the partial exceptions of those few who refused to leave him alone long enough for the template to complete, has run this pattern. He does not know he is running it. He has had it pointed out to him, by Faiza most explicitly, and the file shows him receiving the observation, holding it, and continuing to run the pattern. Insight is present; revision is not. This is not failure of insight or failure of motivation; it is the load-bearing structure of a self that cannot afford to test whether it would still stand if the pattern were modified.

### 6.9 Implications for Surveillance and Understanding

For the purposes of this file the relational pattern yields several operational predictions. He is most vulnerable through his intimates, who form a small and stable set: any intelligence apparatus seeking to model his behavior should map that set with care and update it slowly, as it changes rarely. He is least vulnerable through institutional levers, which he can sever at will. He is approachable, by a figure seeking to be admitted to his trust, only through demonstrated competence, refusal to retreat from his perimeter, and willingness to accept the low-bandwidth terms he can offer. He cannot be befriended by overture; he can be befriended only by endurance.
