# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## Section VI — Moral & Ethical Framework

---

### 1. Preface: Code as Load-Bearing Wall

The subject does not articulate a moral philosophy. Asked directly — and he has been asked, by Harker in the 1970s run, by Faiza Hussain in MI:13, by Doctor Strange across multiple Midnight Sons encounters, by Hannibal King repeatedly across half a century — he tends to deflect into operational language ("there's work to do," "this thing needs killing," "wasn't going to leave her there"). What he refuses to *say* he nevertheless *enacts* with a consistency that is itself diagnostic: the code is too important to expose to language, because language would invite revision, and revision would invite collapse. He does not examine the wall because the wall is what holds the building up.

What follows is the code reconstructed from behavior across fifty years of operational record — the *de facto* ethics, not the homily.

---

### 2. The Hard Rules (Enacted Without Exception Across Canon)

**(a) Vampires die.** This is the irreducible substrate. Across every run — Wolfman, Chichester, Hinz, Mackie, Guggenheim, Cornell, Spurrier, Hill — there is no documented instance of Blade sparing a vampire who is actively predating or who has predated and is unrepentant. The rule predates his knowledge of his own chimerism and survives every revelation about it. It is the first thing he learned in the alley with Afari and it has never been negotiated. When he has hesitated, it has been at the edges of the category (King; Spitfire; Hunter Brawn in some appearances; vampires under coercion or curse), never at its center.

**(b) Children are off-limits in every direction.** He will not kill a child vampire without exhausting other options first, and he will not permit a child — human or otherwise — to be used as bait, leverage, or collateral. This is shown most explicitly in the Hill run's treatment of vulnerable bystanders and in the MI:13 arcs around Faiza's family. The rule extends to his refusal, across every run, to recruit minors into his work. He was nine in the alley; he knows what that does.

**(c) He does not feed.** The Thirst is constant and the prohibition is absolute. The single sustained breach in the canon — the Morbius conversion — is treated by the subject himself, in subsequent narration, as the worst thing that has ever happened to him, worse than any of the four-plus impalements, worse than Afari's death. The serum is acceptable; living donors are not; even consenting donation he has refused in at least two documented instances (a Nightstalkers-era offer from King; a Hill-era offer from a paranormal contact). The rule is not pragmatic — synthetic blood would carry no operational penalty — it is identarian. To feed on a person, even with consent, would collapse the line that constitutes him.

**(d) He does not lie to allies in the field.** Operational deception against enemies is unrestricted; deception against people fighting alongside him is essentially absent from the record. He withholds — extensively, almost pathologically — but the act of stating a falsehood to a teammate registers as a different category and he does not cross it. This is the trait Quincy Harker eventually came to trust him for, and it is what allowed Pete Wisdom (a professional liar) to extend him a working relationship in MI:13. Wisdom's read, paraphrased: *he won't tell you anything, but what he does tell you is true.*

**(e) He finishes what he starts.** Once he has accepted an obligation — to clear a nest, to escort a witness, to hunt a particular target — he completes it or dies trying. There are no documented instances of voluntary abandonment of a contracted task. He has *left* relationships, teams, and cities, but never an active job. This is the discipline that separates him, in his own internal taxonomy, from the predator: the predator opportunistically pursues and abandons; the hunter completes.

---

### 3. The Soft Rules (Strongly Enacted, Occasionally Stretched)

**(a) Humans are not killed.** Strongly held, but the canon shows fracture points. Familiars — humans who serve vampires willingly — he will kill if they are actively combatant, and he has expressed (Chichester run, Guggenheim MAX run) decreasing patience over the decades with the legal-moral distinction between the vampire and the human who knowingly enables predation. His position has hardened: in early Wolfman appearances he disabled familiars; in the Guggenheim MAX and Hill runs he has been observed to kill them outright when they presented active threat. This drift is one of the few measurable shifts in the moral profile across time.

**(b) Civilians are protected at personal cost.** Consistent. He has accepted impalement, exsanguination, and burn injury to extract non-combatants. The rule is not "minimize civilian casualties" (a utilitarian formulation); it is closer to a deontological prohibition on the use of bystanders as means. He will not, for example, allow a civilian death to occur for tactical advantage even where the calculation would favor it. This was a recurring tension in the Mighty Avengers period.

**(c) He does not torture for information.** Intimidation yes; physical coercion within a narrow window yes; sustained torture, no. The distinction in his behavior is functional — he will hurt a vampire to make it talk and then kill it; he will not extend the hurt past the talk. The canon is quietly consistent on this and it is one of the points that separates him from operatives like Wisdom, whose methods he has visibly disapproved of without articulating the disapproval.

**(d) He does not work for money against conscience.** He has taken paid work across the record (the bounty-hunter framing recurs from the 1990s on), but the canon shows him walking away from jobs whose targets he judged unjust, and accepting no fee in cases involving the vulnerable. The economic logic of his life is sustaining-not-accumulating; he lives lean, caches resources for the work, and does not appear to value money beyond instrumentality.

**(e) Mystical and supernatural non-vampire entities are judged case-by-case.** He has worked with witches, werewolves (the Werewolf by Night relationship across multiple runs), ghosts, the magically dead, and inhuman entities. The category of "predator" is functionally narrower than "supernatural"; he applies the predator test (does this thing kill people to live?) rather than the species test. This is a significant moral discipline given his trauma profile and is evidence that the worldview is more sophisticated than he performs.

---

### 4. The Justifications (Such As He Offers Them)

He almost never offers them. When pressed, the formulations are short, almost liturgical, and repeat across decades with minor variation:

- *"They feed on people."* — Used to terminate ethical debate; the entire moral argument compressed into a sentence.
- *"Somebody has to."* — Used to dismiss recognition or thanks; the work as obligation, not virtue.
- *"I know what they are."* — Used to assert epistemic authority over those (including allies) who entertain ambiguity about a target.
- *"Not while I'm here."* — Used in protective contexts; the closest thing in his idiolect to a vow.

The notable absence is theological or metaphysical justification. He does not invoke God, fate, destiny, or higher purpose. He does not, despite the Afari inheritance and the proximity to figures like Faiza (devoutly Muslim) and Strange (mystically engaged), articulate a religious frame. The work is justified by the work; the predator's existence is justification enough for the predator's death. This is morally minimalist in a useful sense — it makes the code portable across contexts and resistant to ideological hijack — but it also means he has no doctrinal apparatus to fall back on when the code is challenged in edge cases. He white-knuckles those instead.

---

### 5. Consistencies — The Code's Spine

The remarkable feature of the file, viewed longitudinally, is how *little* the operational ethics have moved across fifty years of publication and across vastly different writers, editorial regimes, and continuity adjustments. The constant elements:

- The protection of children and non-combatants.
- The refusal to feed.
- The refusal to torture past the information threshold.
- The completion of accepted obligations.
- The protection of intimates at any personal cost.
- The non-exploitation of the vulnerable for tactical advantage.
- The case-by-case treatment of non-vampire supernatural beings.
- The disinterest in personal gain.

That this much can be enumerated and reliably predicted across half a century is itself a finding. The subject is, ethically, one of the most stable figures on the Marvel intelligence board. He is not a moralist; he is a man who has decided what he will and will not do and has stopped revisiting the decision.

---

### 6. Fractures — Where the Code Bends or Breaks

**(a) The Frost exception.** When Deacon Frost is the operative target, the code does not break but it *narrows.* Resources that would be applied to protection or finishing-the-job become subordinated to the Frost pursuit. Allies have on multiple occasions been left in the field while he chased Frost-adjacent leads. He does not lie to them, but he goes. The Wolfman run shows this explicitly; the modern reframings reproduce it. This is the single most reliable degradation point in the file.

**(b) The Switchblade dissociation.** Under the Chichester-era dissociative episode he committed acts — including the apparent killing of innocents — that he would not have committed in integrated state. He has never fully reckoned with the memories. The avoidance is a moral failure he tolerates because integration would be destabilizing; this is the largest unacknowledged debt on the ledger.

**(c) The hardening regarding familiars.** As noted, the willingness to kill human servants of vampires has expanded over decades. The justification is utilitarian (they enable predation; the predation is the harm), but the drift is real and the subject has not, in any documented narration, examined it. This is the area in which the code is most quietly migrating without his oversight.

**(d) The vampire-allies problem.** Hannibal King and Spitfire are categorically vampires; the rule (a) above would, applied without exception, require their destruction. He manages this by individual exception rather than by category revision — King is *Hannibal*, not a vampire; Spitfire is *Jacqueline*, not a vampire. The reasoning is not articulated and would not survive articulation; it is held in place by personal regard. This is the most psychologically interesting fracture, because it shows that the code is more porous to *love* than the subject's self-presentation admits. He cannot revise the category; he can only smuggle individuals out of it.

**(e) The team-leaving pattern.** He repeatedly accepts obligation to a team, completes the immediate operation, and then withdraws — Harker's cell, the Nightstalkers, MI:13, the various Avengers iterations, the Midnight Sons. There is a soft rule he is breaking each time, having to do with sustained loyalty to a collective. He justifies it operationally ("the work is elsewhere"), but the deeper truth is that staying would require the kind of intimacy he cannot tolerate. The code-fracture is hidden inside an attachment problem.

**(f) Self-care as moral category.** He does not consider his own preservation a moral concern except instrumentally (he must function to do the work). This produces decisions that, in another agent, would read as suicidality but in him are better described as a categorical exclusion of the self from the protected class. The hard rule about protecting non-combatants does not, in his application, include himself. This is the fracture he is least likely to ever acknowledge.

---

### 7. Drift Over Time — The Longitudinal Shape

**1970s (Wolfman / Colan, *Tomb of Dracula*).** The code is essentially complete from first appearance: vampires die; civilians are protected; the personal vendetta against Frost is openly acknowledged. Affect around the code is warmer — the early Blade is verbally engaged, banters about the work, expresses something close to pride in his proficiency. The ethics are essentially craftsman-ethics: he does this job, he does it well, he does it because it needs doing and he is good at it.

**1990s (Chichester, *Nightstalkers*, *Blade* solo titles).** The vampirization arc and the Switchblade dissociation force the code into contact with its own underside. The subject emerges from this period with the ethics intact but the affect notably cooler and the relationship to his own nature darker. The Thirst becomes an explicit moral burden rather than a managed condition. The serum-as-discipline emerges as a daily ethical act rather than a medical compliance.

**2000s (Guggenheim MAX; Cornell MI:13).** Two divergent registers. The MAX-era subject is colder, more tactically remorseless, more willing to kill familiars; the Cornell-era subject is, in the company of Faiza and the British team, the warmest version of the character in decades. Both are continuous with the spine. The MAX run shows what the code looks like with the intimates stripped away; the MI:13 run shows what it looks like with intimates briefly available. The code does not change; the *affect around it* tracks the social environment closely.

**2010s–2020s (Spurrier, Hill, ensemble appearances).** Settled into a weary professional register. The code is unchanged. The subject is more willing to acknowledge — to himself, occasionally to others — that the life it constitutes is costly. There is a faint, very faint, opening toward the question *what happens after*, which earlier-era Blade would not have entertained. He does not pursue it.

The shape of the drift, then, is: ethics stable, affect cooling, self-knowledge slowly deepening, willingness to articulate any of the above essentially nil. The wall is the same wall. He has gotten older standing next to it.

---

### 8. The Code's Function for the Self

The final analytic point: the moral framework is not, for this subject, primarily about the world. It is about him. Every hard rule is a wall against the question *am I what I hunt.* The refusal to feed is the wall against the chimerism. The refusal to torture is the wall against the pleasure-in-killing that vampires take. The protection of children is the wall against the night his mother died. The protection of intimates is the wall against the Afari moment repeating without him being able to act. The completion of obligations is the wall against the predator's opportunism. The non-exploitation of the vulnerable is the wall against the Frost moment that began him.

The code is, in this sense, autobiographical in negative — a point-by-point inversion of the predator's profile, lived as an answer to the question the subject has been carrying since he was conscious enough to ask it. He is moral because being moral is how he stays himself. Strip the code and the chimerism is just biology; with the code, the chimerism is the *condition of a chosen life.* He will not let it be stripped.

This is why the code is so resistant to argument and so consistent across decades: it is not an opinion he holds. It is the shape of the wound, hardened into a working surface, on which he has built everything he is.


## Communications & Linguistic Profile

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## Section 6 — Communications & Linguistic Profile

---

### 6.1 Substrate: The Voice Itself

Before register, before content, the file must document the instrument. The subject's speaking voice is a low baritone, produced from the chest rather than the throat, with a deliberate slowing of cadence that is not natural to him — childhood recordings (the few panels of him as a boy in the *Tomb of Dracula* flashbacks and Wolfman's later retellings) imply a quicker, higher London-street pitch that he has spent his adult life suppressing. The current voice is *constructed.* It is the voice of a man who learned, somewhere between Afari's death and his first decade hunting alone, that a slower, lower delivery does three things simultaneously: it reads as authority in any room he enters cold; it conceals dialectal origin (he will not be placed by accent on a single continent); and it conserves breath, which matters to a man whose nervous system is permanently in tactical-arousal baseline and who therefore cannot afford to spend air on inflection.

Volume is calibrated low — consistently below the room's ambient. This forces interlocutors to lean toward him, which (a) gives him micro-data on their attention, balance, and intent, and (b) inverts the usual social geometry: he does not project to be heard; others adjust to hear him. It is a small dominance behavior performed without expression. He raises volume only in three documented contexts: combat coordination at distance, Frost-adjacent confrontations, and the moments — rare — when an intimate is about to walk into harm he can see and they cannot.

Breath control is exceptional. He does not sigh. He does not audibly inhale before speaking. The standard human respiratory tells of grief, frustration, or hesitation are absent from his speech almost entirely, which produces in listeners the consistent reported impression that he is "calm in a way that feels wrong."

---

### 6.2 Dialectal and Code-Switching Profile

The substrate accent is mid-Atlantic, weighted toward American urban inflection but with residual British vowel-shapes that emerge under fatigue, intoxication (rare), or the early phases of Thirst. The Wolfman *Tomb of Dracula* run renders him with an actively American slangy register — "jive turkey," "sucker," "daddy-o" period-marked — which the subject himself appears to have curated as protective coloration during his Soho-to-Boston-to-New-York period; later writers (Chichester, Guggenheim, Spurrier, Hill) drop the period slang and present a stripped, neutral register, which the file reads as the same protective instinct updated for contemporary anonymity. He sounds, deliberately, like he is from nowhere.

He code-switches across at least the following registers, fluidly and without transition-marking:

- **Street/operational vernacular** in low-end urban environments — clipped, contraction-heavy, profanity used as punctuation rather than intensifier.
- **Clinical-tactical** with professional peers (Wisdom, Fury historically, Strange) — noun-heavy, verbless fragments, no adjectives.
- **Folkloric/occult** with practitioners (Strange, the MI:13 mystics, Harker historically) — surprisingly precise terminology drawn from Romanian, Wallachian, ecclesiastical Latin, and Yoruba sources; he will say *strigoi* or *moroi* where another hunter would say "vampire," and he is correct each time about which is meant.
- **Soft register** with Faiza Hussain, with children, with non-combatant witnesses — slower still, simpler diction, shorter sentences, and a notable rise in second-person address ("you're alright," "you're alright now," repeated as a rhythm rather than an assertion).
- **Combat-Frost register** — the only one in which the constructed voice partially collapses. Pitch rises a quarter-step, rate accelerates, contractions disappear, and the residual London comes back into the vowels. This is the single most reliable affective tell in the entire file.

He has functional fluency in conversational Romanian, kitchen French, transactional Spanish and Cantonese, and ritual-Latin reading competence. He has never been observed performing any of these languages for status; he uses them at the lowest register required to complete the operational task and then drops back to English. In *Hunt for Wolverine: Mystery in Madripoor* and the Hill run he is shown understanding conversations in languages he does not acknowledge speaking — a deliberate intelligence behavior.

---

### 6.3 Diction and Lexical Patterns

The standing lexicon is **Anglo-Saxon-weighted, mono- and disyllabic, verb-forward.** He prefers the older, blunter word in nearly every binary pair: *kill* over *eliminate*, *blood* over *hemoglobin*, *hunt* over *pursue*, *dead* over *deceased*, *cut* over *incise*. Latinate vocabulary appears only when the operational situation requires precision (the occult/folkloric register above) or, diagnostically, when he is *evading* — abstraction is one of his concealment strategies, and a sudden polysyllabic turn in his speech is a tell that the topic has touched something he does not intend to discuss directly.

**Pronoun habits.** He uses the first person sparingly. Where another speaker would say "I think we should," he says "we should" or, more often, "go." Where another would say "I'm fine," he says "fine," or nods. Self-reference, when it occurs, is usually in the context of role rather than person: *I hunt,* not *I am a hunter.* He almost never uses possessive pronouns about people — *my partner, my friend, my woman* are absent from the entire fifty-year record. The closest he comes is a flat naming: *King. Faiza. Jamal.* This is not coldness; it is the refusal to perform a possession he does not believe he is entitled to.

**Articles and modifiers.** He drops articles in the operational register ("Got two in the back room") in a way consistent with military speech, but the pattern predates any documented military service and appears to be Afari-trained — the speech of men who shared close quarters and could not afford ambiguity. Adjectives are rare and load-bearing when they appear; if he describes a vampire as *old*, the listener should understand that the vampire is centuries old and that the conversation has just become more dangerous.

**Numbers and time.** He is unusually precise about numerical and temporal references. "Three of them, two doors, ninety seconds" is recognizably his cadence. He does not round. This is partly tactical habit, partly chimerism — his sensory acuity produces actual rather than estimated counts — and partly an aesthetic preference for the thing as it is.

**Profanity.** Used as cadence-marker and emphasis-distributor rather than as expression of affect. He swears more in the street register and almost not at all in the soft register or in Faiza's presence (a tell of respect she has earned without his ever stating it). He does not blaspheme, even casually — a residue of Afari's churchgoing influence that he has never examined.

---

### 6.4 Verbal Tics, Rhythms, and Micro-Patterns

Across runs the following recurring micro-features are documented or reliably inferable:

- **The single-word confirmation.** "Done." "Clear." "Go." Used in place of complete sentences whenever the operational situation permits. Frequency rises with stress; under maximum stress he speaks almost entirely in monosyllables.
- **The two-beat reply.** When asked a question he intends to answer, he pauses approximately two seconds — long enough that interlocutors often begin to rephrase, at which point he answers over the rephrasing. This is partly auditory acuity (he is processing more of the room than the speaker is), partly intelligence behavior (the pause yields tells from the questioner), and partly the older defense of a man who learned not to speak first.
- **The deflected agreement.** Where assent is required socially but not meant, he produces a flat "Mm" or a single nod. He almost never says "yes" without meaning it; conversely, "no" is delivered cleanly and without softening.
- **The name-drop as punctuation.** He uses the addressee's name at the end of a sentence rather than the beginning — *"Stay behind me, Faiza,"* not *"Faiza, stay behind me."* This places the name in the position of weight and tells the listener that the instruction is meant for them specifically and is not negotiable. It is one of the most consistent rhythmic features across all writers.
- **The understated arrival line.** Entrances are marked, when marked at all, with a flat declarative — *"I'm here,"* *"That's mine,"* *"Wrong room."* The Wolfman era allowed more flourish; the modern voice has compressed this to near-haiku.
- **The completed thought left unfinished.** He frequently stops a sentence one beat before its semantic completion, leaving the listener to supply the obvious end. *"You go in there, you don't —"* The omitted *come out* is the point. This is a teaching habit (Afari-derived; the listener who completes the sentence has internalized the lesson) and a refusal-to-name habit (some things he will not put into the air).
- **Absence of filler.** No "um," no "uh," no "like," no "y'know," no "I mean." The absence is itself audible in extended conversation and contributes to the unsettling stillness others report.

---

### 6.5 Rhetoric and Argument Style

He does not argue in the ordinary sense. The standard moves of dialectical exchange — premise-laying, qualification, concession, escalation — are largely absent. His rhetorical default is **assertion-and-wait.** He states the operational fact as he sees it, in one or two sentences, and then stops. If the interlocutor disagrees, he listens through the disagreement without interruption, and then either (a) restates his original position unchanged, (b) accepts the correction in a single word ("Fine"), or (c) acts unilaterally and lets the result settle the question. He does not persuade. He does not negotiate his read of a threat.

When he does extend into longer speech — which happens perhaps once per major arc — the structure is almost always **narrative-procedural**: he tells what happened, in order, with the affect stripped, and lets the events carry the argument. The Faiza scenes in MI:13 contain the longest sustained speech-acts in the modern canon, and they are explanations of mechanism (*how vampires die, why this one will not, what we will need*) rather than expressions of position.

Under hostile interrogation he employs **tactical literalism** — answering exactly the question asked, no more, no less, and forcing the questioner to know what to ask. This is also his preferred move with bureaucratic authority (S.H.I.E.L.D. debriefs, MI:13 intake, court appearances in the Hill run): he produces an unhelpful surface compliance that yields almost nothing while remaining technically cooperative.

Sarcasm and dry humor are present throughout but used surgically. The Wolfman-era quip ("Looks like the party's just getting started, sucker") has been pruned across decades into a flatter modern form, often a single deadpan observation about an absurdity in the situation. The humor is almost always *at the situation's expense*, rarely at a person's, and never at a vulnerable person's. It functions as affect-regulation (he discharges tension through it) and as connection-bid (he uses it almost exclusively with intimates and trusted peers — the appearance of dry humor in his speech to a given individual is itself a status indicator about how he reads them).

---

### 6.6 Deflection Language and Concealment Behaviors

The subject's evasive repertoire is extensive and characteristically *minimalist* rather than elaborate. Where a typical evader generates noise, he generates silence.

- **Topic redirection by operational pivot.** Asked about himself, he answers with the mission. Asked about the past, he answers with the present threat. Asked about feeling, he answers with action. The pivots are not awkward — they are seamless, and most interlocutors do not notice the question went unanswered until later.
- **Subject-position deletion.** "Got handled" instead of "I handled it." "She died" instead of "I lost her." Removing himself from the grammar of the sentence is the most consistent linguistic marker of affectively loaded content. Forensic note: in any transcript, hunt for missing first-person subjects; that is where the wound is.
- **The factual reframe.** Emotional questions are answered with technical facts. "How do you feel about Frost?" yields "Frost is in Marrakesh." The reframe is not deflection-as-refusal but deflection-as-translation — he is genuinely answering the only version of the question he knows how to answer.
- **The walk-away.** Where verbal deflection fails, he leaves. Mid-sentence if necessary. This has been documented in nearly every team-context run and is one of his only socially costly behaviors; he accepts the cost.
- **Operational truth-telling.** Crucially, he does not lie about substantive matters to allies. He omits, he redirects, he goes silent — but the file contains essentially no instances of him telling a direct lie to someone he respects. This is a moral commitment that doubles as an intelligence asset: his word, when given, is reliable, which is operationally valuable and personally non-negotiable.

The one domain in which he reliably *under*-discloses is the Thirst. He will not raise it. He will not name it in mixed company. If pressed he produces the shortest possible factual answer and changes subject. The shame-affect attached to the dependence (Section 2, Section 4) routes through linguistic suppression first.

---

### 6.7 How He Communicates Love

He does not say it. The phrase "I love you" does not appear in the canonical record in his voice. This is a constitutive absence, not an oversight.

Love-communication occurs through four substitute channels, each documented across multiple runs:

1. **Positional protection.** He places his body between the loved person and the threat. The placement is the sentence. With Faiza this is near-constant; with Spitfire it is mutual and therefore particularly visible (each repeatedly steps in front of the other, a small ongoing dialogue in motion).
2. **Operational generosity.** He gives the loved person the kill, the credit, the choice, the better weapon, the safer angle. He does not announce these gifts and would be uncomfortable having them named.
3. **The name, used as address.** Discussed above. When he uses an intimate's name aloud — and he uses it rarely — it is doing the work that "I love you" does in other people's speech.
4. **The grant of presence.** Allowing himself to remain in a room with the person when no operational reason compels it. Sitting. Not speaking. The MI:13 scenes contain several such tableaux with Faiza, in which the communicative act is the choice not to leave.

A fifth, rarer channel: **the disclosed fact.** When he tells an intimate something true about his past — Tara, Afari, the Thirst — the disclosure is the love-act. He does not frame it as such. The frequency of such disclosures with any given individual is the truest measure of his attachment to them. By that measure, his deepest documented attachments in the modern era are Hannibal King and Faiza Hussain, in that order.

---

### 6.8 How He Communicates Threat

The threat-register is the most economical part of his communication and the most studied by adversaries who survive their first encounter.

- **The named distance.** "I'm coming." Or, more chillingly, the location-specific variant: "I know where you sleep." These are not boasts; they are operational reports delivered to the target in advance, and they are accurate.
- **The reduction to mechanism.** Threat is communicated by describing what will happen in flat procedural terms — *"I will find you. I will take the head. I will burn what's left."* The procedural register removes negotiation as a category; one does not negotiate with a procedure.
- **The use of stillness.** Threat is escalated not by raising volume but by ceasing to move. The voice drops further. The pause before each phrase extends. Interlocutors consistently report that the *quietest* moment is the most dangerous, which is correct.
- **The single-word terminal.** "Don't." "Stop." "No." Delivered flat, without modifier. Compliance rates among adversaries who have heard this from him are reportedly high; non-compliance has been uniformly fatal.
- **The Frost-specific exception.** Frost-directed threat collapses the discipline. Speech becomes rapid, profane, personal, and explicitly emotional in ways absent from every other context. This is the only documented circumstance in which he names what he feels (*"I'll kill you for what you did to her"* and variants) — and the naming is itself the warning that the standard operating envelope no longer applies.

He does not bluff. The file contains no instance of a threat issued that was not subsequently executed when the conditions for execution obtained. This is a long-cultivated reputation and a moral commitment: the threat, once spoken, *is* the act in advance.

---

### 6.9 How He Communicates Grief

He does not. Or rather: grief in his communication appears only as **absence, structure, and ritual.**

- **The unnamed dead.** He almost never says the names of those he has lost. Tara is referenced as "my mother" in the rare instances she is referenced at all; Afari is "Jamal," used sparingly and only with those who knew him; the lovers who turned and were killed are not named in subsequent runs at all. The withholding of the name is the mourning.
- **The operational anniversary.** He marks dates by being where the loss occurred or by hunting on the date. The behavior is observable across decades — the recurring returns to Soho, the specific cemetery visits, the timing of certain Frost-pursuits to dates that map back to the original murder. He does not call them anniversaries. He simply moves.
- **The structural sentence.** When grief must be addressed verbally — usually because another character has raised it — he produces a short, structurally complete declarative that contains the fact and nothing else. *"She's gone."* *"He turned. I did what was needed."* The completeness of the sentence is itself the containment.
- **Somatic discharge.** Grief that cannot be spoken is metabolized through training, hunting, and the long solitary walks documented across multiple runs. The walks are, in effect, his prayer.
- **The single permitted gesture.** Across the entire canon, he has been observed exactly a handful of times performing a small physical ritual — touching a blade to his forehead, a brief closed-hand pause, the placing of a hand flat against a wall at a site of loss. These are not displayed. They occur when he believes himself unobserved. They are the closest thing in the file to overt mourning.

He has never been documented weeping in language or on the page. The file should not interpret this as the absence of grief; it is the *form* the grief has taken, which is structural rather than expressive. The man is, in linguistic terms, a cenotaph — a marker over an absence.

---

### 6.10 Tells: How to Read Him

A surveillance file's most valuable section is the tell-set. The following are the reliable linguistic and paralinguistic indicators across the longitudinal record:

- **Vowel-shift to London** → fatigue, Thirst-onset, or Frost-stimulus. The constructed voice is the first thing to go.
- **Loss of first-person subject** → the topic has touched a wound. Note what was being discussed.
- **Polysyllabic / Latinate turn** → he is concealing. The abstraction is doing work the silence cannot.
- **Cessation of dry humor with a specific person** → either he has revised his read of them downward (now untrusted) or the situation has escalated past the register in which humor functions. Cross-reference with proximity behavior to disambiguate.
- **Use of the addressee's name terminally** → the instruction is non-negotiable and the named person is, at minimum, tactically valued; at maximum, loved.
- **Two-beat pause extending to four or more** → he is making a decision the answer to the question depends on, and the decision is not primarily about the question.
- **Sudden silence mid-conversation** → his auditory or olfactory threshold has been crossed by something the other party cannot perceive. Stop talking; follow his eyes.
- **Walking away without closing the exchange** → the conversation had reached a topic he would not address verbally. Do not pursue. Resume later on operational ground.
- **Rapid, profane, personal speech** → Frost or Frost-coded stimulus. Tactical judgment is degraded; do not rely on his read of the situation until the stimulus is resolved.
- **The flat procedural threat-sentence** → the threat will be executed. Plan accordingly.
- **The disclosed biographical fact, unprompted** → the listener has just been granted a status he does not give easily and would not name. Do not remark on it. Do not refer to it later unless he raises it first.
- **The granted presence without speech** → the same status, in a different modality. The silence is the conversation.

---

### 6.11 Summary Read

The communications profile is, in the end, of a piece with everything else in the file: a system built for survival by a man who learned early that words could neither save the people he loved nor return them, and who therefore allocated language strictly to the functions it could perform — coordination, warning, the small precise rituals of operational care. He has compressed himself into the smallest possible verbal footprint compatible with continued function, and inside that footprint there is, for those who can read it, a complete affective grammar: love as positioning, grief as structure, threat as procedure, attachment as the use of a name. He will not, in this life, learn to speak more openly than he does. He has already chosen the language he can survive in. The file should be read with that choice respected.


## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## Predictive Model I — Routine & Social

---

The following predictions are derived from the behavioral substrate established in Sections 1–5: disorganized attachment with dismissive overlay, vocational sublimation, hypervigilant somatic baseline, managed metabolic dependence, and a self-concept organized around the paradox of being the cure for the disease he carries. Each prediction is framed in the GIVEN → EXPECT form an intelligence apparatus would use to model the subject's behavior in domains the published record does not directly depict. Granularity is calibrated to the level a surveillance file would actually contain: which seat, which hand, which window, which silence.

---

### I. DOMESTIC ROUTINE & SOLITUDE

**GIVEN** he has acquired a new safe-flat or operational base, **EXPECT** within the first ninety minutes: a full perimeter walk (interior, then exterior), identification and mental flagging of every line-of-sight from facing windows, removal or covering of mirrors in any room where he will sleep (the mirror-test is a vampire detection heuristic he has internalized as habit and as a check on his own reflection — both readings apply), and the seating of at least two edged-weapon caches at non-obvious chokepoints (behind the refrigerator kickplate; under the lip of a bathroom counter). Bed will be placed so that the door is visible from a supine position and the window is not behind his head. Curtains will be heavy and double-layered, not for sunlight (he tolerates it) but to deny silhouette.

**GIVEN** he wakes in an unfamiliar room, **EXPECT** a 1.5–3 second eye-only sweep before any postural change — pupils tracking ceiling-to-corners-to-door — followed by an inhale held long enough to inventory scents. He does not stretch on waking. He sits up in a single controlled motion, feet to floor, weapon-hand free. Time from REM to combat-ready is under four seconds and has been since adolescence.

**GIVEN** he is alone in a residence for more than forty-eight hours, **EXPECT** the following ritual structure to emerge: serum dose at fixed intervals (predicted near-twelve-hour spacing, dawn and dusk by preference — the symbolism is not incidental, but the timing is also metabolically optimized); weapon maintenance daily, conducted as a near-meditative practice with the components laid out on a cloth in a fixed left-to-right order; physical conditioning twice daily, low-equipment, repeatable in any environment (calisthenics, shadow-bladework, breathing drills); one full sensory decompression period of roughly twenty minutes in which he sits motionless with eyes closed, which a naive observer would read as rest and which is in fact a deliberate exercise in dialing down the hypervigilant baseline enough to prevent burnout.

**GIVEN** he cooks for himself, **EXPECT** spartan, protein-dense, repetitive — the same three or four meals on rotation, prepared without recipe, eaten standing or at a counter facing the entry. He does not linger at table. Cleanup is immediate; a dirty knife in a sink is an unsecured weapon and a tell to anyone who enters.

**GIVEN** he has unstructured time and no immediate operational pressure, **EXPECT** he will fill it with low-yield productive activity rather than recreation: re-honing blades that do not need honing, re-checking caches he checked yesterday, reading occult or tactical material with a pen in hand. Television is unlikely. Music is possible and specifically likely to be mid-century jazz — Afari's register; this is the single sentimental tell in his domestic life and he would not be able to explain it if asked. He does not own pets. He does not keep plants. Neither would survive his operational tempo and he knows it.

**GIVEN** a power outage in his residence, **EXPECT** no behavioral change whatsoever. His night vision renders it a non-event. He will not light candles. He notes the outage as a tactical fact (silent alarm systems compromised; neighbors distracted) and proceeds.

---

### II. THE SERUM AND THE THIRST

**GIVEN** scheduled dose time, **EXPECT** a fixed sequence: hands washed, dose drawn or uncapped, brief held inhale before ingestion, dose taken in a single motion without ceremony, container immediately secured or destroyed. He does not look at the substance while taking it. He does not look at himself in any reflective surface during the act. Total elapsed time: under thirty seconds. He resents the duration.

**GIVEN** he is in a location where his supply will not be accessible for more than seventy-two hours, **EXPECT** pre-positioning of at least three redundant caches along his projected route, geographically dispersed, in formats that read as innocuous (a medical-supply blister in a first-aid kit, a flask in a vehicle, a sealed vial taped inside a book). He maintains a mental map of every cache he has ever placed and culls those older than a year.

**GIVEN** a missed dose by four hours, **EXPECT** subtle behavioral signature: marginally increased irritability, a tendency to stand closer to walls, micro-tremor in the non-dominant hand suppressed by clenching, increased frequency of olfactory checks (head-turns toward scent sources he would normally filter). He will not mention it.

**GIVEN** a missed dose by twelve hours, **EXPECT** active withdrawal-management behaviors: physical exertion to displace ideation, withdrawal from contact with civilians (he will excuse himself or relocate), avoidance of any environment containing accessible human blood (no hospitals, no abattoirs, no contact sports). Speech becomes shorter. Eye contact decreases.

**GIVEN** the substance is offered to him by anyone other than himself or a fully trusted medical intimate, **EXPECT** refusal regardless of need. The supply chain is a vulnerability he controls or does not use.

**GIVEN** he is offered alcohol in a social setting, **EXPECT** acceptance of one drink (whiskey by preference, neat), held more than drunk, used as a social prop. He will not finish it if attention turns elsewhere. He will never accept a second from the same pourer in the same evening.

---

### III. MOVEMENT THROUGH PUBLIC SPACE

**GIVEN** he is walking a city street, **EXPECT** a consistent micro-pattern: pace slightly faster than ambient, path biased toward the building-side of the sidewalk (sightlines longer, ambush angles reduced), head still while eyes track in a regular sweep pattern (forward, left mirror-check via shop windows, right mirror-check, forward). At every intersection he pauses a half-step longer than the crossing signal requires, using the pause to inventory the cross-street. He does not use phone or earbuds. He carries nothing in his dominant hand.

**GIVEN** he enters any indoor public space, **EXPECT** a sub-second scan in the threshold pause: exit count, exit positions, occupant count, occupants flagged as armed/anomalous/predatory, lighting sources, reflective surfaces usable as indirect sightlines. He will move to a seat or standing position that places his back to a wall, his face to the primary entry, and a secondary egress within four steps. If no such position exists he will stand rather than sit.

**GIVEN** a restaurant or bar, **EXPECT** order placed quickly and without consultation of the menu (he has pre-decided), payment in cash, tip generous and round-numbered (forgettable, no card trail, no memorable behavior), departure within a tight window. He will not face away from the door for the duration of the meal. He will not eat anything that requires both hands.

**GIVEN** public transit, **EXPECT** preference for rear or end-car seating, standing if the car is crowded enough to compromise reaction lanes. He does not sleep on transit. He clocks every boarding passenger in the first two seconds they enter his car and re-clocks at every stop.

**GIVEN** he is being followed by a single competent surveillant, **EXPECT** he identifies the tail within two to four city blocks. He will not confront. He will lead the tail through three or four route changes designed to confirm, then make a decision: lose them via a pre-mapped break-pattern (an alley, a building with multiple exits, a transit transfer) if they are merely curious; identify and prosecute them if they read as a vampire-aligned asset.

**GIVEN** a crowded venue (concert, stadium, market), **EXPECT** visible physiological cost — jaw set, micro-frequency increase in scan rate, deliberate breath-pacing to suppress the involuntary predator-screening his nervous system performs on every face. He will tolerate this for the duration of a mission. He will not tolerate it for entertainment. He has not voluntarily attended a public spectacle in decades.

---

### IV. SOCIAL ENCOUNTERS WITH STRANGERS

**GIVEN** a stranger initiates small talk (cashier, bartender, fellow waiting passenger), **EXPECT** minimal, polite, deflective responses delivered in a register pitched to terminate the exchange without offense. Eye contact is brief and direct, not warm. He uses honorifics ("ma'am," "sir") more than his apparent age and register would suggest — a holdover from the era of his formation and a tool for managing distance without rudeness.

**GIVEN** a stranger flirts with him, **EXPECT** he registers the approach with a half-second longer eye contact than the deflection pattern allows, then deflects anyway. If the flirt is from someone reading as a civilian human, the deflection is gentle and final. If the flirt is from someone whose scent or affect carries any of the anomalous markers that constitute his attachment profile (chimerism, supernatural exposure, the caregiver register), the deflection is slower and may not fully take.

**GIVEN** a child addresses him directly, **EXPECT** a marked softening — voice dropped slightly, posture lowered, eye contact longer and more patient than with adults. He will answer questions truthfully within reason. He will not initiate contact with children but he will not refuse it. This is one of two domains where the constricted affect briefly opens.

**GIVEN** a person in visible distress (lost, injured, in danger) in his vicinity, **EXPECT** intervention proportional to need and inversely proportional to witnesses. He will help. He will not stay to be thanked. He will give a false name if asked.

**GIVEN** he is asked for his name, **EXPECT** a cycling roster of operational aliases keyed to the context. "Eric" is given only to those he has decided to trust over a period of months or longer. "Brooks" is rarer still. "Blade" is the public-facing operational identity and he uses it only with those already inside the world he operates in.

**GIVEN** he is photographed without consent, **EXPECT** he registers the act in real time (he tracks lenses the way he tracks weapons), and depending on context either ignores it (tourist, harmless), interposes a hand or turn (journalist, civilian curious), or follows up later to secure the image (hostile or surveillance context). He does not destroy phones in public. He locates them later.

---

### V. CONVERSATION AND VERBAL HABIT

**GIVEN** any extended conversation, **EXPECT** more listening than speaking by a ratio of roughly three to one. He asks short questions. He does not interrupt. He uses silence as a tool more deliberately than most interlocutors recognize — a held pause after another's statement frequently elicits more disclosure than a follow-up question would. This is partly trained interrogation craft and partly the default of a man who finds speech costly.

**GIVEN** he is asked a direct question about his past, **EXPECT** one of three responses calibrated to the questioner: a flat factual sentence stripped of affect ("My mother died when I was born"); a redirection delivered as dry humor; or silence held long enough that the questioner moves on. The choice is conscious. The selection criteria are the questioner's standing and the operational relevance of the answer.

**GIVEN** he is lied to, **EXPECT** he identifies the lie in real time (micro-expression, scent shift, vocal stress) and does not call it out. He logs it, adjusts his model of the speaker, and continues the conversation as though nothing had happened. The speaker has been demoted in a register that will not be made visible until it operationally matters.

**GIVEN** he gives a compliment, **EXPECT** it is technical and specific — about a teammate's marksmanship, a tactical call, a piece of fieldcraft. He does not compliment appearance. He does not compliment character in language. The presence of any such compliment in his speech is a significant data point and indicates a relationship that has moved past the operational frame.

**GIVEN** he must deceive an adversary in conversation, **EXPECT** competent, low-affect deception built on truths shifted one or two degrees. He does not enjoy it. He does not invent flourishes. He exits the deceptive frame as quickly as the operation permits.

**GIVEN** he is teased or mocked by a trusted peer, **EXPECT** he absorbs it with a flat half-smile and a brief return volley that is drier than the original. This is the second domain where the constricted affect briefly opens. With Hannibal King in particular the verbal register thaws further than with anyone else in the record, and we predict this generalizes — peer-banter with proven intimates is the closest he comes to recreational speech.

---

### VI. WORK, MONEY, AND LOGISTICS

**GIVEN** the question of income, **EXPECT** a layered solution: bounty work in the supernatural-adjacent economy (vampire-cult assets seized in raids and liquidated through occult-network fences), contract retainers from institutional clients (MI:13-style or private), and a deep base of accumulated wealth from a century of operations that he treats as quartermaster supply rather than personal fortune. Cash, gold, and bearer instruments in multiple caches across multiple cities. No central bank relationship beyond the minimum required for operational legitimacy.

**GIVEN** he must produce identification, **EXPECT** a stable of three to seven working legends maintained with discipline — passport, supporting documents, biographical cover thin but consistent. The legends are functional, not deep; he does not method-act them. He uses each just long enough to burn it appropriately and rotates.

**GIVEN** he must travel internationally, **EXPECT** preference for ground and sea over air where time permits, because air travel concentrates him in an environment with poor egress and no weapon. When he must fly, he flies with serum in pharmaceutically labeled containers and weapons shipped ahead through pre-positioned channels. He is meticulously polite to customs officers.

**GIVEN** he must rent a vehicle, **EXPECT** mid-tier, common make, dark color, manual transmission if available (greater control, fewer electronic failure modes). He adjusts mirrors before adjusting the seat. He does not use GPS audio. He has memorized the route.

**GIVEN** he must communicate operationally, **EXPECT** preference for in-person, then for dead-drops and pre-arranged signal protocols, then for voice on burner devices, with text as a last resort and email essentially never. He distrusts the substrate of all electronic communication and treats every digital channel as compromised by default.

**GIVEN** he is offered a long-term institutional position (S.H.I.E.L.D. liaison, MI:13 permanent posting, Avengers reserve roster), **EXPECT** initial acceptance contingent on operational necessity, followed within twelve to twenty-four months by quiet departure when the institutional friction exceeds the operational gain. The departure pattern is predictable enough across the canon to be a near-law: he leaves before the institution can either absorb or expel him.

---

### VII. SLEEP, REST, AND THE BODY OFF-DUTY

**GIVEN** he sleeps, **EXPECT** four to six hours, polyphasic when operations permit (two segments of two to three hours rather than a single block), light enough that any door-handle pressure wakes him fully. He does not dream that he can recall, or claims not to; the canon's silence on this is probably accurate to his self-report rather than to his actual sleep architecture, which we would predict includes regular trauma-pattern dreams that he has trained himself not to retrieve on waking.

**GIVEN** the question of sex, **EXPECT** rare, episodic, and almost exclusively with partners who fall inside the narrow attachment topology described in Section 3 — anomalous, capable, situationally embedded. He is not promiscuous; the operational and somatic costs of intimacy with strangers exceed any benefit. When sexual encounters do occur they are framed in operational time (during an extended joint mission, at the resolution of a shared crisis) and end without sentimental aftermath he is willing to acknowledge, though the predicted internal cost is significant and is metabolized through subsequent withdrawal and increased operational tempo.

**GIVEN** illness or injury below the threshold requiring assistance, **EXPECT** complete concealment from all observers. He will modify gait to hide a limp, breathing to hide a chest wound, expression to hide pain. The healing factor permits this. He treats his own wounds in private with practiced efficiency.

**GIVEN** illness or injury above that threshold, **EXPECT** he accepts care from a narrow list of vetted practitioners (occult-medical specialists, the few mainstream physicians read into his chimerism), tolerates the process in near-silence, and resumes operations as soon as ambulatory rather than as soon as recovered. He is a bad patient by the standards of any practitioner who values follow-through.

**GIVEN** a designated rest day enforced by an ally, **EXPECT** he honors the letter of the agreement and violates the spirit — he will not work the case, but he will train, maintain, study, and pre-position. Genuine idleness is intolerable for reasons that connect directly back to the Thirst and the intrusive content it produces when his attention is unoccupied.

---

### VIII. INSIDE A TEAM

**GIVEN** he is integrated into a team for the duration of a mission, **EXPECT** the following arc: first 24–72 hours, perimeter-of-the-group positioning, minimal disclosure, careful threat-modeling of each teammate as if they could turn (because in his experience they could); next phase, established positional role in fights (point or flank, never center, never command unless thrust upon him), willingness to take the risk-positions others would balk at; mid-mission, dry humor begins to surface with whichever teammate proves trustworthy first; resolution, quiet departure before debrief if it can be managed.

**GIVEN** a teammate is wounded, **EXPECT** immediate triage-grade competence (decades of field medicine), no verbal reassurance beyond what is operationally necessary, and a marked shift in his subsequent engagement of whoever caused the wound — colder, more methodical, lethal where lethality is permitted.

**GIVEN** a teammate questions his methods, **EXPECT** he hears the question fully, answers briefly if the questioner has standing, and disregards if they do not. He does not argue. If the disagreement is operationally serious he will execute the team's plan and then act on his own judgment when the team cannot see.

**GIVEN** he is given orders by a commanding figure, **EXPECT** compliance proportional to competence as established earlier. He will not perform deference. He will not perform insubordination either. His salute, if forced to give one, is correct and unsentimental.

**GIVEN** a teammate attempts to befriend him with persistence and warmth (the Faiza pattern), **EXPECT** initial deflection, gradual softening over weeks, eventual acceptance of a role he himself would call protective rather than affectionate, and an internal cost in attachment-fear that he manages by increasing operational distance whenever the bond approaches a threshold he cannot tolerate. The relationship will survive precisely because the other party keeps reaching across that distance.

---

### IX. CONTACT WITH CIVILIANS AND THE PROTECTED

**GIVEN** he encounters a civilian witness to a vampiric event, **EXPECT** rapid de-escalation in voice and posture, clear short directives ("Don't look. Walk to that corner. Stay there"), competent reality-management afterward (he will not lie about what they saw, but he will frame it in terms they can carry), and a follow-up check days later that they will not realize was a check.

**GIVEN** a civilian thanks him, **EXPECT** discomfort visible only in a brief failure of eye contact, a nod, and immediate movement to terminate the exchange. Gratitude is not a register he can metabolize.

**GIVEN** he must interact with the family of someone he failed to save, **EXPECT** attendance if his presence is requested and would not endanger them, silence at the wake, a single sentence offered if pressed, and a private commitment to the case that he will not name as such. He attends funerals of his dead. He does not speak at them.

**GIVEN** a former intimate whose life he extracted himself from contacts him, **EXPECT** he responds. He never initiates. The response will be operationally framed even when the contact is not.

---

### X. SOMATIC TELLS AND MICRO-PATTERNS A SURVEILLANCE FILE WOULD CONTAIN

The following are predicted signatures consistent enough to constitute identification markers independent of disguise:

- A consistent right-hand bias in weapon draw and a left-hand bias in non-dominant tasks (door handles, payments), suggesting practiced ambidextrous compartmentalization rather than true ambidexterity.
- A standing posture with weight slightly forward on the balls of the feet, knees unlocked, never fully at rest in any environment that includes other people.
- A swallow reflex visible at the moment of any blood-scent encounter, suppressed within a second by deliberate breath control. This is the single tell he has not fully trained out and probably cannot.
- A consistent half-second pause before entering any threshold, regardless of how familiar the space.
- A habit of touching the haft of a concealed blade as a self-soothing check at moments of cognitive transition (waking, finishing a conversation, before sleep). He is not aware he does this.
- Speech volume calibrated approximately one notch below ambient — a forcing function that makes interlocutors lean in and quiet themselves, with the secondary benefit of denying nearby surveillance clean audio.
- Eyes that do not track moving objects continuously but in discrete saccades on a regular cadence — a scanning pattern rather than an attending one, even in conversation.
- Total absence of fidgeting. No tapping, no pen-clicking, no leg-bouncing, no jewelry-touching. Stillness as baseline. When stillness breaks, it is to act.
- A characteristic exhale before any committed physical action — combat, the dose, sleep, departure. The exhale is the demarcation between intention and execution and is observable enough to be a tell for a sufficiently attentive adversary.

---

### XI. THE PREDICTED OFF-DUTY SELF (NEGATIVE SPACE)

The canon's silence on his recreational life is itself data. Predictions in the negative:

He does not have hobbies in the civilian sense. He does not collect. He does not garden. He does not write. He does not travel for pleasure — every journey is a route. He does not celebrate his own birthday and likely does not know it precisely (perinatal-loss cases often carry this gap). He does not observe holidays except as operational variables (Halloween crowd dynamics; Christmas-Eve church attendance increasing certain hunting grounds). He does not maintain a residence he would call home; he maint


## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## Predictive Model II — Crisis, Betrayal & the Wound

---

The predictions below are derived from the substrate established in Sections 1–5: the perinatal mother-loss, the Afari recursion, the Frost-fixation, the chimeric metabolism and the Thirst, the disorganized-dismissive attachment topology, the constricted-affect CPTSD profile, and the narrow exception-set of permitted intimates. Each entry takes a stimulus condition and projects the most probable behavioral output, with the granularity an exhaustive surveillance file would record — micro-cues, escalation thresholds, the recovery curve afterward, and where the model could fail. The predictions cluster around five vectors: acute combat crisis; betrayal by an ally; sexual or emotional temptation; the Thirst and serum-supply emergencies; and direct strikes against the wound itself.

---

### I. Acute Combat & Operational Crisis

**GIVEN** a sudden ambush in an unfamiliar interior — narrow corridor, unknown number of hostiles, civilian present —
**EXPECT** an immediate triangulation between exit, civilian, and nearest weapon-of-opportunity completed inside the first second; movement toward the civilian rather than the exit; the civilian placed at his off-shoulder and walked backward toward a structural choke; verbal output reduced to two-to-four-word imperatives ("behind me," "stay down," "left"); blade drawn underhanded along the forearm rather than en garde, so the first cut is a counter rather than an opening; he will accept the first hit if it positions him for the second strike. Pulse and respiration do not visibly elevate. The recovery debrief afterward will omit any reference to his own injuries unless directly asked.

**GIVEN** an operation going catastrophically wrong — intelligence proven false, multiple allies down, primary target escaping —
**EXPECT** the field decision to triage toward extraction of the wounded over pursuit, even when pursuit is tactically correct; he overcorrects on this axis specifically because Afari's death is the template he refuses to repeat. He will personally carry the most badly wounded body and will not delegate this. He will be the last to leave the room. In the post-action review he will accept disproportionate blame, refuse offered exculpation, and within seventy-two hours will have planned an unsanctioned solo return to complete the original objective.

**GIVEN** outnumbering at a ratio he assesses as terminal (canonically demonstrated against vampiric hordes; modern equivalent ≥ 12:1 with hostiles capable of wounding him) —
**EXPECT** no surrender behavior of any kind; instead a methodical recalibration toward maximizing damage-per-second and protecting his back against a vertical surface. He will speak less, not more. Tactical humor disappears entirely above approximately 8:1; below that ratio it is a regulation cue and can be relied upon as a baseline indicator of his actual stress level. The complete absence of the dry register in a high-density engagement is the surveillance flag that he believes he is dying.

**GIVEN** capture and restraint by a competent adversary —
**EXPECT** an initial period — minutes to hours — of complete behavioral inertness, during which he is cataloguing restraints, guard rotations, ambient sound, scent inventory of his captors (vampire/human screen completed within seconds), and structural weaknesses. He will not speak first. He will not respond to interrogation with information but will respond with calibrated noise designed to extend the interaction and gather data. Pain compliance fails on him both because of his pain threshold and because pain returns him to a familiar interior state. Threats to him personally are inert; threats to a named third party will produce the only genuine affective response a captor is likely to observe, which is precisely why he will refuse to acknowledge any named third party as mattering to him, and why a captor who *correctly* names an intimate will see him go briefly, dangerously still.

**GIVEN** a teammate behaving recklessly in the middle of an engagement —
**EXPECT** a single sharp verbal correction; if ignored, no second correction; instead a silent repositioning to cover the predicted error. He does not lecture in the field. Post-action he may say nothing for hours, then deliver one sentence at the end of the debrief that the teammate will remember for years. He does not write people off for one error. He writes them off for the second.

---

### II. Betrayal

**GIVEN** discovery that an ally has been feeding intelligence to the adversary —
**EXPECT** no immediate confrontation. He will verify independently and exhaustively (the dismissive-attachment overlay makes him slow to credit betrayal precisely because he half-expects it and does not want to act on the expectation alone). Verification window: 48–96 hours of parallel surveillance. During this window his behavior toward the suspected ally will be indistinguishable from baseline to anyone but a trained observer; the tells are a one-beat lengthening of eye contact and a refusal to turn his back in shared rooms. Upon verification: a single private meeting, no weapons drawn, the evidence laid out flat, and an offered choice — walk away from the work, or be walked away from it. Killing the betrayer is reserved for the case where the betrayal has produced a death he holds them responsible for. He has a separate, harsher protocol for betrayers who lied about a vampiric affiliation.

**GIVEN** discovery that an intimate (King-tier, Faiza-tier, Spitfire-tier) has been compromised — turned, possessed, blackmailed, or coerced —
**EXPECT** an immediate categorical shift in which the intimate is reclassified as a *rescue objective* rather than as a betrayer. He will resist every attempt by other allies to treat them as a threat. He will accept extraordinary personal and operational cost to extract them. If extraction proves impossible and the intimate must be killed, he will insist on doing it himself, will do it cleanly, will not speak for approximately seventy-two hours afterward, will not eat (serum dosing maintained, food refused), and will work alone for the following six to twelve weeks. He will not attend any ritual of mourning. The Afari template runs underneath this entire sequence and he knows it does.

**GIVEN** institutional betrayal — S.H.I.E.L.D./MI:13/Avengers-adjacent body using him as expendable asset, withholding intel, or scapegoating him for a sanctioned operation —
**EXPECT** no protest, no appeal, no public statement. He will complete the current operation, deliver a terse formal severance, and disappear from the institution's reach inside seven days. He will not return to the institution under the same leadership. He will continue to work *with* individual members of the institution who he assesses as personally trustworthy, treating the institution itself as discarded. This pattern is documented across every team affiliation in his fifty-year file and is the single most reliable institutional prediction in the dossier.

**GIVEN** a betrayal that is itself a manipulation — i.e., an ally was framed, and the apparent betrayal is the adversary's construction —
**EXPECT** the verification protocol to save him from premature action, but the residue of the false betrayal will permanently degrade the relationship. He does not fully restore trust once it has been operationally withdrawn, even when the withdrawal is proven unjust. This is a known structural limit and he is aware of it; the awareness does not change the limit.

---

### III. Temptation — Sexual, Emotional, Affiliative

**GIVEN** a sexual approach by an ordinary human woman of no operational relevance —
**EXPECT** a courteous, brief deflection; he is neither performatively chaste nor available. If the approach persists across a sustained encounter (single mission, single location) he may permit a single-night exception, will leave before dawn without contact information exchanged, and will not return. The internal accounting is that he has not exposed her to his world. There is no observed pattern of repeat contacts with the same civilian partner. The deflection register is markedly gentler than his deflection of any other class of social overture; this is the one place in the file where his voice softens predictably.

**GIVEN** a sexual or romantic approach by a partial-vampire or vampire-adjacent woman of operational competence (the Spitfire template) —
**EXPECT** he will not deflect. He will not pursue either. He will become available across a longer arc — months of shared work — and will permit the relationship to form by accretion rather than by decision. Verbal declarations will be minimal to absent. Physical tenderness will be present but rationed. He will exit the relationship at the first credible operational pretext, will frame the exit as duty, and will return periodically without acknowledging the pattern. He will protect her with disproportionate ferocity in any field situation and will pretend this is professional.

**GIVEN** an offer of cure — a procedure, magical or technological, that would eliminate the Thirst and the chimeric metabolism —
**EXPECT** prolonged silence, refusal to discuss in the moment, and a delayed decision that almost always declines. The refusal is psychologically over-determined: the chimerism is the operational basis of his vocation; removing it would remove him from the work and there is no observed self that exists outside the work; additionally, the cure would symbolically sever him from the mother-event, which is the only relationship he has with her. He does not articulate any of this. The articulated reason will be tactical — "I'd be less useful." A sufficiently insightful offerer who pressed on the second layer would be met with hostility disproportionate to the prompt and the conversation would end.

**GIVEN** an offer of full vampiric power without the moral cost — bargained surrender to a faction promising he could retain his targeting discretion —
**EXPECT** flat refusal, no deliberation, no curiosity. This is the one temptation he is structurally immune to because accepting it would invalidate the founding decision; the entire personality is the refusal of this offer made repeatedly across decades. An adversary who leads with this offer reveals they have not read him.

**GIVEN** an offer of family — adoption into a found-family team-structure, a permanent home base, a stable cohabitation arrangement with an intimate —
**EXPECT** participation up to approximately six to eighteen months, increasing micro-withdrawals across the latter half of that window (longer field absences, returned-from-mission delays, rooms slept in alone when shared rooms are available), and a triggering event — usually a near-loss of one of the family — that he uses as occasion to leave. He will leave gently, with explicit care for the people involved, and will remain on call for them indefinitely. He will not return as a member. This is the Quincy Harker / Nightstalkers / MI:13 pattern; it will repeat.

**GIVEN** an offer to know more about his mother — recovered records, a surviving witness, an occult method of communicating with her —
**EXPECT** the strongest involuntary affective response in his repertoire short of the Frost-trigger. He will hide it. He will pursue the offer cautiously and alone, will not tell his closest allies, and is at his most manipulable in this window. A fabricated mother-contact is the single highest-yield manipulation vector against him in the file. The illusion-of-mother variant has been attempted in canon and produces protracted disorientation and, on at least one read, the closest thing to a tactical breakdown he displays outside the Switchblade episode.

---

### IV. The Thirst & Serum Crisis

**GIVEN** routine daily dosing, on schedule, supply secure —
**EXPECT** the dose is taken in private, never in the presence of allies if it can be avoided, often in a bathroom or a vehicle, with a brief held-breath stillness afterward that an intimate observer would read as the only ritual moment in his day. Resupply is performed on a rotating schedule across multiple caches (the surveillance prediction is that he maintains a minimum of four geographically separated caches at any time, with at least one in a jurisdiction he is not legally present in). Cache inventory and rotation are tracked obsessively; this is the only domain in which he is observably compulsive.

**GIVEN** a missed dose by ≤ 12 hours —
**EXPECT** no observable degradation. He has trained against this margin. Internally there is heightened salience of blood-associated stimuli, which he suppresses.

**GIVEN** missed dosing at 24–48 hours —
**EXPECT** the first observable cues: a fine tremor in the off-hand suppressed when noticed; a one-beat latency in conversational response; pupillary dilation in low light; an increased frequency of his own scent-checks of the room (a brief inhalation through the nose he is mostly unaware of); refusal of food. He will not disclose the state to allies unless directly asked by an intimate he trusts to manage it. The shame register is engaged from approximately hour 30.

**GIVEN** missed dosing at 48–96 hours —
**EXPECT** intrusive ideation regarding feeding becomes continuous; he begins to avoid civilian-dense environments deliberately; voice flattens further; the tremor extends to both hands and is no longer suppressible; he will eat raw meat as a partial substitute and will be observed doing so with self-disgust; he will isolate; if operating with a team he will request relief and will accept restraint protocols if they are pre-arranged. He will not initiate a request for restraint, but he will not resist a competent offer.

**GIVEN** dosing failure beyond approximately 96 hours under combat conditions —
**EXPECT** graduated loss of the discrimination between hostile and non-hostile blood-bearing bodies; tactical effectiveness paradoxically increases in the short window before it collapses, because the predator-screening of crowds becomes uninhibited; he will retreat from civilian areas if any executive function remains. The construction of pre-arranged restraint protocols with at least one trusted intimate is the standing standing-order of his life; an adversary aware of this could attempt to sever the restraint arrangement before inducing the crisis.

**GIVEN** an adversary destroying his cache network in coordinated fashion —
**EXPECT** the recognition of the pattern is immediate (he checks at least one cache daily; the pattern is visible inside 72 hours). Response is to consolidate to the most secure cache, contact the chemist or supplier he trusts, and accept operational pause. He will not steal serum from a medical facility unless no alternative exists. He will not feed on a willing donor as a bridging measure unless the alternative is uncontrolled crisis; the willing-donor option has been canonically present in his world (Hannibal King, certain serum-derived substitutes from controlled donors) and his refusal of it is psychologically diagnostic — it would compromise the line.

**GIVEN** forced feeding — i.e., blood introduced into him under coercion —
**EXPECT** the most severe shame response in the file, lasting weeks. He will withdraw from intimates rather than let them see the recovery. He will overcompensate operationally afterward, taking missions of higher risk than warranted, until the affective load has been discharged through action. This is the foreseeable adversary play and the one he has the least defense against.

---

### V. Direct Strikes Against the Wound

**GIVEN** the introduction of Deacon Frost into a current scenario —
**EXPECT** immediate and reliable degradation of strategic judgment. Tactical execution remains sharp; *target selection* narrows pathologically. He will pursue Frost at the cost of secondary objectives. He will accept ambushes obviously structured around the Frost-bait. Allies who have worked with him for any length of time know to physically interpose or to misdirect intelligence about Frost's location when the larger operation requires it; he will recognize the misdirection in retrospect and will accept it without grudge if the larger operation succeeded. The Frost-trigger is the one operational liability he himself acknowledges, in the canonical record, as a known fact about himself.

**GIVEN** any presentation of his mother — illusion, photograph he has not previously seen, audio reconstruction, an apparent witness who claims to have known her —
**EXPECT** complete operational pause. He will demand verification with a precision he does not apply to other intelligence. He will conduct the verification alone. During the verification window he is dangerously manipulable in adjacent domains because his attention is monopolized. A counter-prediction: he is *more* skeptical of mother-presentations than of any other category of intelligence, because he has been targeted with them before; the manipulator must be exceptionally credible or must approach obliquely. The Dracula-class adversary has the resources to do this; lesser adversaries who attempt it produce only rage.

**GIVEN** an adversary articulating the *am-I-what-I-hunt* question aloud, with sophistication —
**EXPECT** silence, not engagement. He does not debate the question because debating it would dignify the proposition that it remains open for him; the answer has been operationally settled by the entire shape of his life and to discuss it would re-open it. The silence is not avoidance; it is closure. A sufficiently long sustained pressure on this question (captivity-scale, days) would produce one of two outcomes: a hardened reinforcement of the founding refusal, or — under serum deprivation simultaneously — a brittleness that approaches the failure mode. Dracula has approached this and has been refused; lesser adversaries have approached it and have been killed.
