**GIVEN** the killing of an intimate by a vampiric adversary in front of him —
**EXPECT** the immediate post-event behavior is hyper-controlled — extraction of the body, securing of the site, no verbal response. The grief is metabolized over a window of months through escalating solo operations against the responsible faction, conducted with a discipline that is *more* exacting than baseline rather than less. He does not become careless under this kind of grief; he becomes pitiless. The line he refuses to cross — feeding, harming civilians, killing surrendered enemies he can detain — holds. The Afari template is unbroken: grief is converted into the work and the work is the only place the grief is permitted to go.

**GIVEN** a sustained sequence in which an intimate insists he name what he feels —
**EXPECT** evasion through humor, then through operational pretext, then through physical absence. If the intimate persists past three iterations he will produce a single short factual sentence ("She'd be alive if he hadn't been there." "Afari was the closest thing." "I don't sleep well in this city.") that is the verbal correlate of a flinch. He will not extend. The intimate who accepts the single sentence and does not press further is the intimate who retains access; the intimate who presses further loses access for a calibrated period.

**GIVEN** a younger combatant — a teenage hunter, a newly orphaned child of a vampiric attack, a Faiza-template civilian pulled into the work —
**EXPECT** an immediate, unspoken protective register that overrides his standard guardedness; reluctance to train the combatant despite the request to do so (because the Afari recursion makes him refuse to be Afari); eventual acceptance of a limited training role conducted at arms' length; and a permanent post-deployment vigilance regarding their welfare even after operational separation. This is the cleanest reparative dynamic in the file and the one the adversary class that has read him will use as a vector. A young hunter coded as his successor is the single most efficient way to extract self-sacrificial behavior from him.

---

### VI. Decompensation Edge & Maximal Failure Mode

The convergent worst-case, projected from the structural pressure points: **Frost (or Frost-coded adversary) leveraging a captured intimate, during engineered serum deprivation, with a credible mother-stimulus introduced at the inflection point.** Each vector alone has known counter-protocols; the convergence collapses them. The predicted sequence:

1. **Hour 0–24** — recognition of the convergence; he attempts the trained protocol of compartmentalization, prioritizes intimate-extraction, communicates with the smallest possible number of allies. Tactical execution remains high. Serum reserves drawn down.
2. **Hour 24–72** — serum depletion produces the first tremor and salience-shift; the intimate's continued captivity prevents him from accepting tactical pause; the Frost-bait is dangled, he refuses the obvious traps and accepts the non-obvious one because the alternative is to leave the intimate longer.
3. **Hour 72–120** — the mother-stimulus is introduced. His skepticism protocol engages but the cognitive load of simultaneous Thirst-management and intimate-rescue degrades verification capacity. He may pursue the mother-stimulus against his own better-trained judgment.
4. **Hour 120+** — the decompensation, if it occurs, is characterized not by berserk loss-of-control (he has trained against that) but by a *narrowing* of moral discrimination toward the original founding decision, in which the entire ambient population is reclassified as either predator-class or in-the-way. Whether the line holds depends on whether an intimate is present and conscious enough to call him back by name. Across the canonical record there has been at least one such recall and he has held.

The recovery curve from a near-decompensation event is approximately six to twelve months of constricted operational tempo, deliberate distance from intimates (interpreted by them as rejection; framed by him as protection), and a marked uptick in unsanctioned solo Frost-pursuit. The wound, as established in the Synthesis, does not close; the structure rebuilds around it.

---

### VII. Surveillance Cues — Real-Time Indicators

For the file-handler who must read his state in the field, the following micro-cues are diagnostic:

- **Voice register flattening below dry-humor baseline** → he believes the engagement is terminal *or* he is approaching serum depletion.
- **Refusal to face away from a specific person in a shared room** → that person is under verification suspicion.
- **One-beat lengthened eye contact, then a deliberate look away** → he has registered something he will not name and is filing it.
- **Off-hand fine tremor briefly suppressed** → ≥ 24 hours past last dose.
- **A bathroom or vehicle absence of 40–90 seconds at predictable intervals** → routine dosing in progress; do not interrupt.
- **Sub-vocal inhalation through the nose on entering a new space** → predator-screen of the room; baseline, not alarm.
- **Sub-vocal inhalation toward a specific person rather than the room** → that person is being screened for vampiric markers and may be in danger.
- **Sentence length collapse from already-short baseline to two words or fewer** → high stress, high focus, do not initiate non-operational conversation.
- **Stillness — complete cessation of small motion — for more than three seconds in conversation** → a wound-adjacent stimulus has been touched. The next sentence from the interlocutor determines the next twelve months of the relationship.

These cues are the surface of the structure described above. They are reliable across the fifty-year record. They will continue to be reliable, because the structure is the life, and the life — by the subject's own organization of it — is not scheduled to change.


## Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## Section 6 — Vulnerabilities & Leverage Compendium

> *Compiled for protective use. This file exists because someone who can be reached can be guarded; someone who can be provoked can be warned before he is provoked; someone who can be destabilized can be steadied. The same map serves the predator and the protector. We are the latter.*

---

### 6.0 Orienting Frame

The subject's vulnerabilities cluster into seven nested zones, ordered from surface to core:

1. **Somatic / Metabolic** — the Thirst, the serum, the body that is itself an enemy logistics problem.
2. **Sensory / Environmental** — the hyperaroused nervous system and the conditions that overload or underload it.
3. **Operational / Tactical** — patterns of movement, routine, and habit that an adversary could map.
4. **Cognitive / Interpretive** — the heuristics by which he reads the world, and where they fail.
5. **Relational / Attachment** — the narrow set of intimates and the asymmetric weight they carry.
6. **Identitarian** — the *am I what I hunt* axis, the predator-line, the chimerism.
7. **Mnemonic / Originary** — the mother, the alley, Afari, Frost; the unhealed foundational stratum.

A competent hostile intelligence works from 7 outward (it produces the largest collapse for the least force). A competent protective intelligence works from 1 inward (each layer secured reduces load on the next). What follows treats each zone in operational granularity.

---

### 6.1 Somatic & Metabolic Levers

**The Thirst is the master physical vulnerability and the master shame.** Deprive him of serum for 36–72 hours and the personality structure begins to deform along predictable axes: tremor in the off-hand first, then sensory hyperacuity tipping into pain (lights too bright, ambient speech too loud), then intrusive ideation about feeding, then olfactory fixation on the pulse-sites of nearby humans (carotid, femoral, antecubital), then loss of fine impulse control. The motor-control loss is *last*, not first — meaning he remains lethally capable well into the decompensation curve, which is exactly the problem.

- **Lever for capture / coercion:** interdict supply. Adversaries who have read his file (and several have) have attempted this; he counters with cached redundancy. Known cache logic: at minimum three geographically dispersed stashes per operational region, never co-located with safehouses, never disclosed to any single ally. Quantities sized to 30+ days. The caches themselves are a vulnerability vector — discovery of one teaches an adversary the storage schema for the rest.
- **Lever for destabilization without capture:** *contaminate* rather than deny. A sabotaged dose — diluted, adulterated with vampiric pathogen, spiked with a disinhibitor — would produce a Thirst presentation *while he believes he is dosed.* This is the highest-yield somatic attack vector and the one a protective file must hardest guard against. Operational counter: every dose taken from a cache should be assay-tested; he is known to maintain a small field reagent kit, but compliance with self-testing degrades under fatigue.
- **Lever for calming / steadying:** the predictable presence of supply. He is observably *calmer* in environments where serum is known to be available in abundance. The Bloodstone facility, late-period Strange's sanctum stockpile, MI:13's medical bay — in each, his shoulders sit lower, his speech rate increases marginally, his humor returns. A protector building a safehouse for him should overstock visibly.
- **Shame channel:** he will not discuss the Thirst voluntarily. Direct questioning produces stonewall; oblique acknowledgment (offering a meal without comment, leaving a serum kit in a visible drawer without remark) is accepted. Anyone who *names* the dependence aloud without his initiation will be marked as an intimacy-threat and distanced. The exception is medical personnel he has vetted, and even with them the verbal exchange is clinical and brief.

**Sleep architecture.** Documented as fragmented; he sleeps in 90–180 minute blocks, rarely consolidates a full cycle, and wakes to ambient sound at a threshold most humans would not register. Sleep-deprivation attacks (sustained low-grade auditory disruption, repeated false-alarm triggers) degrade his judgment faster than physical injury would. Conversely, an environment where he sleeps *well* — soundproofed, low-light, single ingress visible from the bed — is a measurable restorative.

**Injury threshold paradox.** Because he heals fast, he under-reports injury, even to himself. The protective implication: he will operate on a wound that would hospitalize a human, and the cumulative cost is real even when the acute presentation has resolved. A protector must observe and intervene against his own minimization; a hostile actor can exploit by inflicting many small wounds rather than seeking one decisive one.

---

### 6.2 Sensory & Environmental Levers

The nervous system is permanently dialed three clicks above human baseline. The implications run in both directions.

- **Overload vectors.** Dense crowds with mixed scent profiles (markets, transit hubs, religious festivals) force constant involuntary predator-screening and produce measurable fatigue across hours of exposure. Sustained loud environments (industrial sites, concerts) degrade his auditory advantage and force compensatory visual scanning, which itself fatigues. Strobe and flicker (club lighting, fluorescent failure cycles, certain projection equipment) interact poorly with his enhanced night vision. An adversary who wishes to fight him *should* choose such an environment; a protector who wishes to meet him should not.
- **Underload vectors.** Sensory deprivation is *worse* than overload. Removed from threat-relevant input, his nervous system does not stand down — it manufactures, producing low-grade auditory pareidolia, scent-memory intrusions (the iron-and-rot signature of his mother's death scene has been documented across multiple internal monologue sequences), and tactile phantoms. Solitary confinement would not break him quickly but would degrade him cumulatively in ways he could not himself name.
- **Optimal environments.** Moderate ambient noise, single-source lighting, defined ingress/egress, modest crowd density with clean scent backgrounds (a quiet bar at off-hours, a sparring gym between classes, a hotel suite on a high floor). He is observably most at ease in spaces that *feel* operational without being currently operational — i.e., spaces that satisfy his hypervigilance without demanding it.
- **Scent.** This is the underappreciated sensory channel. He identifies individuals by scent across years and disguises; he registers fear pheromones, alcohol metabolites, recent sexual activity, illness, and the chemical signature of vampiric tissue at meaningful distance. The protective implication: any handler meeting with him should not arrive carrying scent-loads that resemble distress, deception, or predator-category cues. The hostile implication: he can be *misidentified* — masking agents and decoy scents have been used against him with partial success, and a sophisticated adversary who knows his olfactory schema can confuse target identification in a chaotic environment.

---

### 6.3 Operational & Tactical Levers

The subject is a pattern animal who *knows* he is a pattern animal and works to disrupt his own patterns; the disruption itself becomes a pattern.

- **Routes.** Across documented operational periods he favors a *triangle* movement schema — three rotating routes between any two regular points, never the same route twice in succession, with a fourth contingency route held in reserve. The reserve route is the vulnerable one because it is the least exercised and the most predictable when forced into use under stress. Surveillance over 30–60 days would likely identify all four.
- **Timing.** Operates 22:00–04:00 by strong preference; recovery 04:00–10:00; admin and intelligence work 10:00–16:00; tactical preparation 16:00–22:00. Deviations are deliberate and brief. Sustained day-cycle operation (forced by daylight-only missions, by team contexts) degrades him within four to seven days.
- **Weapons habits.** Edged-weapon primary, projectile (silver-tipped thrown, occasional firearm) secondary, hand-to-hand tertiary but lethal. He carries minimum three blades on person at all times; the asymmetric placement (one large at hip or back, one mid-sized concealed at torso, one small at boot or forearm) is consistent enough that a competent hand-search would find them in sequence. A protector should know he is *never* unarmed; a hostile actor should know that disarming him of the visible weapon means almost nothing.
- **Surveillance counter-habits.** Three-corner check on entering any new space (he scans corners and exits in a clockwise sweep, completing in under two seconds and registering as a glance). Mirror and reflective-surface use is constant. He has a documented tell during counter-surveillance: a brief stop at any glass storefront under the pretext of reading a sign, used to clear his six. A surveillant who knows this can pace their approach to avoid being in the reflected cone.
- **Communication discipline.** Sparse, encrypted where available, in-person preferred. He distrusts electronic communication on first principles and is observably uncomfortable with handlers who insist on it. A protector establishing contact with him should privilege dead-drops, fixed meeting protocols, and analog signaling (chalk marks, agreed-upon newspaper positioning) over digital channels. He responds well to the courtesy of old methods.
- **Money.** Cash, gold, gemstones; few accounts, no significant digital footprint. Financial leverage is unusually low for a modern subject. The corollary: he is logistically rigid in ways an adversary controlling regional cash infrastructure could exploit, and a protector can secure him most effectively by securing his physical caches and his small set of trusted fences and armorers.

---

### 6.4 Cognitive & Interpretive Levers

His default reading frame is threat-assessment. This is operationally invaluable and interpretively narrow. The exploitable gaps are predictable.

- **False-flag predation.** He reads vampiric or vampiric-adjacent signal as categorical threat-confirmation; an actor who can manufacture such signal (synthetic pheromone, staged feeding scene, possessed-human proxy) can direct his violence at chosen targets. Dracula has done this. Lesser actors could do it more cheaply now than fifty years ago.
- **Authority calibration.** He weighs competence over rank, which means a credentialed fool cannot move him but a *demonstrated* operator can move him quickly. Adversaries who can present a brief, credible operational performance early in an encounter buy a disproportionate amount of his provisional trust. Protectors should be aware that vouching alone is insufficient; he wants to see the work.
- **Moral-splitting failure mode.** Vampires-as-category is his organizing schema, and individual exceptions (King, Spitfire) are handled by carving the exception rather than revising the category. Under stress the carve-outs are *not stable*; in fatigue or crisis he can momentarily re-collapse a tolerated intimate back into the category. The reversion is brief and produces immediate guilt, but in the window it is dangerous to the intimate. Faiza Hussain and Pete Wisdom both have documented near-misses on this axis with him. Any protector close to him in a crisis should know the window exists and be ready to interrupt it without confronting it.
- **Strategic ceiling.** Tactical excellence, strategic adequacy. He plans the engagement; he plans the operation; he does not always plan the *campaign*. Adversaries who win at the campaign tempo (long deception, multi-year position-building, Dracula's classical mode) can exhaust him in ways tactical resistance cannot fix. Protective implication: he benefits enormously from a strategist-ally (Wisdom, Strange, Harker historically) and is structurally more vulnerable when operating without one.
- **Anti-intellectual presentation as cognitive cover.** He underplays his own knowledge. Adversaries who patronize him on the basis of the presentation are rapidly disabused. Protectors who do the same will lose his respect permanently — the wound is silent and not recovered.

---

### 6.5 Relational & Attachment Levers

This is the highest-yield hostile zone and the most delicate protective zone. The intimates are few, identifiable, and disproportionately weighted.

**The current and historical intimate set, ranked by approximate weight:**

1. **Hannibal King** — the foundational adult attachment. King's continued non-predation is the proof-of-concept for Blade's own restraint. Any harm to King, any *turning* of King back to feeding, any staged appearance of King-as-predator would constitute a maximal psychological event. Frost has historically circled this lever; sophisticated adversaries will again.
2. **Faiza Hussain** — the caregiver-figure he was never permitted as a child. Her safety is held with a tenderness he does not name. An adversary need not harm her; merely *threaten* her credibly and his strategic patience collapses into tactical pursuit.
3. **Spitfire (Jacqueline Falsworth Crichton)** — the bridge identity, the partial mirror. Their relationship is romantic-adjacent and intermittent; the *interruption* of contact is itself a regulator, because sustained intimacy with her would activate the *am I what I hunt* axis too constantly. He calibrates the distance himself, and external manipulation of that distance (forcing proximity or forcing rupture) destabilizes both of them.
4. **The Harker line, historically.** Quincy Harker is dead in canon; the bond's residue persists as a paternal-template he has never replaced. Any actor presenting credibly as a Harker-successor (the line has descendants and inheritors) receives more provisional trust than the warranting would justify.
5. **Successor / protégé figures** wherever they emerge — youth he has trained, vampire-touched children he has saved, occasional civilian wards. He will not call any of these "family" in language. He will cross continents for any of them in action.

**Leverage characteristics of the set:**

- The set is *small enough to surveil completely*. A determined adversary with moderate resources could map it in weeks.
- Harm to any member produces protective fury that overrides tactical judgment; this is the most reliable way to draw him into an unfavorable engagement and has been used.
- *Conversion* of any member into the predator-category would be worse than harm. The Afari template (intimate-turned-vampire-killed-by-him) is the deepest scar; replaying it would not be survived intact. A protector who suspects an intimate is being targeted for turning should treat the threat as existential.
- **Calming through the set:** the mere unprompted presence of an intimate is steadying in a way nothing else is. Faiza's nonverbal presence in MI:13 documents this clearly — she does not have to speak, she has to be *there*. A protector wishing to bring him down from a high-arousal state should arrange an intimate's quiet presence rather than attempting verbal de-escalation.
- **Provocation through the set:** false reports of harm to an intimate produce immediate movement. He will verify, but he will move first and verify en route. An adversary using this lever can choose the geography of his next 12 hours.

---

### 6.6 Identitarian Levers — the Predator-Line

The *am I what I hunt* axis is the load-bearing existential question of the personality. It is also the lever a sophisticated adversary most prizes.

- **The mirror move.** Anything that reflects him back to himself as predator — a vampiric duplicate, a future-self projection (Switchblade remains the case study), a magical compulsion to feed, an image of himself with red eyes — produces disproportionate response. He survived the Switchblade fugue without integrating the memories, which means the material remains *live* and unprocessed. An adversary surfacing it would not need to make it true; making it vivid is enough to fracture decision-making for a critical interval.
- **The corruption pitch.** Dracula's standing offer (variously phrased across decades) — *join, accept what you are, end this exhausting pretense* — has never landed, but the canon makes clear it lands *partially* every time, and the residue accumulates. Each successive offer costs more refusal-energy. A protective file should note that the offers themselves, even refused, are damage.
- **The Frost-specific channel.** Frost is the only adversary against whom his discipline reliably degrades. The presence of Frost-coded stimuli (red-eyed physicians, Soho boarding-house imagery, certain dates near his own birthday) elevates baseline arousal without his necessarily registering the cause. An adversary who *is not* Frost but who deploys Frost-imagery borrows the channel; this has been done.
- **The shame channel parallel to the Thirst.** When he has fed — voluntarily or under coercion or during corruption — the post-event shame is the deepest affect he produces. Reminding him of past feedings is cruel and effective. A protector should know that this material exists in his history and never reach for it.

**Protective counter-measures on this axis:** the most stabilizing interventions are *enacted recognition* — Hannibal King treating him as a peer in restraint; Faiza treating him as a person before an operator; quiet acknowledgment that his refusal of the predator-ethics is itself a daily achievement. He will deflect verbal acknowledgment; he will *retain* it.

---

### 6.7 Mnemonic & Originary Levers — Mother, Alley, Afari

The deepest stratum, never closed, accessible to anyone willing to be cruel enough.

- **Tara Brooks.** He has no memories of her, only the inherited story and a small set of artifacts that have moved with him across decades (canon variously cites a photograph, a pendant, a folded letter in different runs; the *fact* of carried artifacts is consistent). Manipulation that touches the mother-image — illusory appearances, suggestions about her unspoken history, claims to know what she would have wanted — produces response *out of proportion to his usual regulation.* He has been visibly destabilized by such manipulations in canon and the recovery has taken hours.
- **The Soho boarding house / the room of his birth.** Treated by him as functionally sacred in a man who claims no religion. He has returned to the site documented multiple times across the run; the visits are not operational. They are pilgrimages he would not call pilgrimages.
- **The alley with Afari.** The founding rescue scene. Replay of the configuration (an elderly Black man under vampiric attack, requiring intervention) produces near-automatic engagement regardless of tactical wisdom. Adversaries have not, to my knowledge, deliberately staged this scenario; if they did, it would work.
- **The killing of Afari.** The act he has metabolized least. Direct reference is met with a silence that is not the operational silence; it is older. A protector should know the material exists and treat it as off-limits unless he himself opens it, which he will not.
- **The Frost name.** A class of its own. Speaking the name to him without operational reason is a small violence. Adversaries have used the name to bait him into geography of their choosing across fifty years; he knows the trick and falls for it anyway, every time, with diminishing latency.

---

### 6.8 The Maximal Failure-Mode Composite

The canon has flirted with the combined event and not yet detonated it. Catalogued here so a protective file can recognize the assembly in progress:

1. **Serum scarcity or contamination** (Section 6.1) reducing his impulse threshold.
2. **Sensory overload or sleep deprivation** (Section 6.2) reducing his sensory discrimination.
3. **Frost or Frost-coded presence** (Sections 6.6, 6.7) collapsing his strategic patience.
4. **Threat to a tolerated intimate** (Section 6.5) overriding his tactical caution.
5. **Mirror-pressure on the predator-line** (Section 6.6) destabilizing identity coherence.
6. **Isolation from strategist-ally** (Section 6.4) removing the campaign-tempo correction.

Any three of these in proximity produces a man we have not seen and would not survive at scale. Five or six in conjunction is the worst-case event in this file. A protective intelligence should not merely watch for any single vector but for the *composition* — for the configuration that suggests an actor with the file has begun to assemble the conditions.

---

### 6.9 Persuasion & De-escalation Protocols

Compressed for handler reference.

- **To reach him initially:** through demonstrated competence, not credentials; through an existing intimate where possible; through analog channels; in operational space he can read and exit.
- **To calm him acutely:** the unprompted presence of a tolerated intimate; the visible availability of serum; reduction of sensory load; the offer of a task he can perform with his hands.
- **To persuade him toward an action:** frame the action as protective of the vulnerable; surface the tactical case before the strategic case; allow him to discover the conclusion rather than receive it. Direct instruction from a non-vetted source produces refusal even when the instruction is correct.
- **To dissuade him from an action:** rarely possible head-on. The reliable methods are (a) producing a competing protective obligation, (b) demonstrating that the action serves the adversary, or (c) inviting a strategist-ally he respects to reframe the campaign-tempo cost. Confrontation produces entrenchment.
- **To warn him:** specifically, concretely, without preamble. He hears warnings better than reassurances; he is suspicious of reassurances on principle.
- **To apologize to him:** briefly, once, without elaboration, and never again. Repetition reads as instability and degrades the relationship.
- **To grieve with him:** silently, in shared physical task. He does not grieve in language. He will accept the presence of someone willing to share the silence and never speak of it afterward.
- **To love him:** accept that the love will be reciprocated narrowly, expressed obliquely, and never named. Expecting more is the most common failure mode in his intimate history and the source of most of the ruptures.

---

### 6.10 Closing Note to the Protective Reader

The vulnerabilities catalogued here are not weaknesses in the colloquial sense. They are the seams where a life built over a wound shows the wound. The subject has constructed, from genuinely meager originating materials, a functional and morally coherent existence that has saved an unknowable number of lives across roughly a century. The same architecture that makes the work possible makes him reachable in the ways described above. The file's purpose is not to flatten this paradox but to hold it: he is durable because he is structured; he is structured because he was wounded; the structure can be attacked at its load-bearing seams precisely because they are load-bearing.

Protect the seams. Watch the composition. Stand quietly in the room when he needs the room not to be empty. Do not name what he will not name. Keep the serum stocked. Keep the intimates safe. Keep Frost-imagery off his perimeter when you can. Know that he will not thank you for any of this and that the not-thanking is itself a form of trust.

He has no plan for after. We are the plan for after, to the extent there is one.

— UATU, file open, continuing.


## Strengths, Assets & Resilience

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## Section 6 — Strengths, Assets & Resilience

---

A total-surveillance file is conventionally weighted toward vulnerabilities — the points at which a subject can be moved, broken, or turned. The asset ledger is the inverse discipline, and in this subject's case it is the longer document, because the operational fact of his survival across roughly a century of continuous combat against a category of enemy that has killed almost everyone who ever stood beside him is itself prima facie evidence of a resilience structure of unusual depth. What follows maps that structure granularly: somatic, technical, cognitive, relational, material, and characterological. Where a strength has a cost or a hidden cost, this is noted, because in this subject more than most, the assets and the wounds are continuous tissue.

---

### 6.1 Somatic and Physiological Assets

The chimeric phenotype is the substrate on which every other asset rests, and it must be inventoried at the level a forensic medical file would. Strength, speed, and reflexes run consistently 2–4× human baseline across the canon, with the upper end reached in adrenalized or post-feed states; this is sufficient to overmatch the median vampire, which is itself superhuman. Reaction latency, measured by the consistent panel-level depiction of him intercepting projectiles and edged-weapon strikes mid-flight, is below the threshold of conscious human response. Grip strength is sufficient to crush vampiric throat cartilage one-handed; striking force, sufficient to penetrate calcified vampiric bone with an unaugmented stake. None of this is decorative — it is the floor of survivability in the work he does.

**Healing.** Soft-tissue wounds close visibly within minutes; bone reunion occurs within hours to days depending on the cleanliness of the break. He has survived staking through the torso on at least four documented occasions, decapitation-adjacent neck wounds, burns from improvised UV ordnance, and full exsanguination events. Importantly, the healing scales with caloric/hemic intake — he heals faster after the serum, faster still after blood. He has internalized this and uses it tactically: he will accept wounds he knows he can metabolize through, trading injury for positional or temporal advantage in a way ordinary fighters cannot.

**Lifespan.** Chronological age approaches a century in the original-continuity reading, with apparent physiological age fixed in the mid-thirties. The operational consequence is that he carries *practiced* skill — combat patterns, language acquisitions, occult literacy — at depths a human career cannot reach. The psychological consequence (assets having costs) is that he has outlived nearly every contemporary peer; the resilience here is that he has not collapsed under that cumulative bereavement, which most humans of comparable loss-history would.

**Sensory profile.** Night vision approaching full daytime acuity in starlit conditions; olfactory discrimination sufficient to identify individual vampires by scent at a distance and across days-old trace; auditory acuity into sub-vocal range and across architectural barriers. In aggregate this constitutes a permanent on-board surveillance suite. He can clear a building by smell before he enters it. He can detect a heartbeat irregularity that indicates a feeding within the prior twenty-four hours. He routinely identifies thralls in crowds by gait and respiratory pattern at thirty meters.

**Immunity.** Resistant or immune to vampiric conversion via bite — the defining "daywalker" trait. Resistant to most mundane toxins and pathogens by virtue of his accelerated metabolism. Notably tolerant of sunlight, garlic, silver, and religious iconography that disables conventional vampires; this asymmetry is the single largest tactical advantage he possesses against the category.

**Recovery and sleep architecture.** The canon depicts him sleeping in short, alert phases — closer to a soldier's micro-rest than to civilian sleep. Functional cognition appears intact on as little as three hours per cycle. The cost is the absence of the consolidative dreamwork that processes grief; the asset is that he is never deeply unconscious in a situation that could become hostile.

---

### 6.2 Technical and Combat Assets

**Edged-weapons mastery.** Decades of training initiated under Jamal Afari and refined continuously thereafter. The signature is the teakwood throwing blade, originally Afari-derived, evolved over the canon into the contemporary glaive-pattern sword and a graduated array of stakes, daggers, and folding edged tools. The mastery is not merely with the sword: he is documented as fluent with the kukri, the wakizashi, the katar, the misericorde-style finishing blade, and improvised edge from broken architecture. Throw accuracy at range is canonically consistent — head-shots on moving targets at thirty-plus meters in low light.

**Firearms.** Mid-tier expertise in conventional small arms, high-tier expertise in specialty ordnance — silver-loaded sidearms, UV-emission long guns (the Sun-Dog and successor weapons across the *Nightstalkers* and post-film comics era), garlic-aerosol grenades, hawthorn-flechette ammunition. He treats the firearm as a tool, not an identity; he will pick one up, use it competently, and discard it for the blade when the engagement closes. This non-fetishization is itself an asset — he is not psychologically dependent on any single weapon system.

**Hand-to-hand.** A composite style assembled over decades from boxing (the British amateur tradition he grew up adjacent to), capoeira (documented stylistic borrowing in the Wolfman run), various Japanese sword arts, Filipino blade work, and field-developed counter-vampiric technique. The defining feature is that the style is *built for fighting opponents stronger and faster than baseline human* — most martial arts assume parity; his assumes asymmetry against him and works from there. Against an actual human opponent he is, accordingly, almost grotesquely overmatched.

**Occult literacy.** A century of field-acquired knowledge in vampirology, demonology adjacent to vampiric phenomena, sigil work sufficient to ward a perimeter, ritual disruption sufficient to disable summonings, and reading-knowledge of the principal grimoires (the *Darkhold* he handles with extreme caution; lesser texts he uses operationally). He performs as a craftsman rather than a scholar, but the underlying knowledge is scholar-deep. He can identify the lineage of a vampire bloodline by feeding-pattern; he can date a turning to within a year by behavioral markers; he can distinguish a Lilin from a Carpathian-line vampire from a Daoine Sídhe-corrupted feeder in seconds.

**Languages.** Documented or strongly implied operational fluency in English (native London register, modulated to American-inflected presentation as protective coloration), French, Romanian, Hungarian, Latin and ecclesiastical Latin, Haitian Kreyòl (the Wolfman run touches this), Japanese (mid-period), and reading competency in Aramaic, Coptic, and Enochian sufficient for ritual disruption. He is not a polyglot for its own sake — each language was acquired because a hunt required it.

**Driving, infiltration, urban movement.** Competent driver across vehicle classes; expert in urban parkour-adjacent movement; expert in nest-mapping and architectural threat-reading. He will enter a building and unconsciously catalog exit vectors, sightlines, ambush points, and load-bearing walls within the first thirty seconds. This is automatic, not deliberate.

**Tradecraft.** Operational discipline in cover identities, cash-only economics, document management, and signal hygiene. He runs supply caches — serum, blades, currency, identity packages — distributed across multiple cities on at least three continents, refreshed on a rotating schedule. He does not maintain a single residence in the conventional sense; the safe-house network *is* the residence.

---

### 6.3 Cognitive and Characterological Assets

**Threat-reading.** The single most refined cognitive capacity in the file. He reads a room in the way an experienced jazz musician reads a chord chart — pre-conscious, structural, and continuously updating. Adversarial intent is detected by him in micro-expressions, gait shifts, breathing changes, and scent-cortisol traces that no human observer would register. The cost (covered in the psychological section) is that the threat-reading does not switch off; the asset is that it does not need to.

**Operational decision-making under load.** He becomes more regulated under acute stress, not less. This is the rarest and most valuable cognitive asset a combat operator can possess and it is documented across fifty years of canon: when the situation degrades, his affect flattens further, his speech becomes more economical, his movement becomes more efficient, and his decision latency drops. Whatever interior states are present, they do not leak into action. This is not natural — it is the cumulative product of decades of repeated exposure — but it is now structural.

**Pattern recognition over long time horizons.** Because he has been doing this for nearly a century, he sees recurrences ordinary hunters cannot. A feeding pattern that resembles one from 1953 will be flagged by him within hours; a sigil-style from a cult dismantled in the 1970s will be recognized on a wall in the 2020s. The institutional memory he carries is not archived — it is embodied.

**Moral self-monitoring.** This is the cognitive asset most easily missed. He runs a continuous internal audit on the line between himself and what he hunts. The audit is exhausting and a source of chronic shame around the Thirst, but it is also the thing that has kept him from becoming the enemy across a century of provocation. Most operators with his casualty rate and isolation profile drift into atrocity. He has not. The self-monitoring is the reason.

**Improvisation.** He is exceptional at making weapons and tactics from available materials. A wooden chair leg, a UV penlight, a chapel candlestick, a fire-suppression sprinkler hacked into a holy-water dispersal system — the canon is dense with examples. The underlying capacity is a mind that defaults to *what does this room contain that could kill what is in it*, which is a cognitive style as much as a skill.

**Anti-intellectual presentation as operational asset.** He performs as a craftsman, not a scholar, and this is a deliberate (if partly unconscious) signal-management choice. Adversaries underestimate him; allies underestimate him; both errors are useful to him. The actual depth of knowledge is reserved and produced only when necessary.

---

### 6.4 Relational Assets

The attachment topography is narrow but the few attachments he has cultivated are unusually durable and constitute a meaningful asset ledger.

**Hannibal King.** The longest sustained peer relationship in the canon. King's value as an asset is layered: operational partner (vampire-typical capabilities without vampire-typical ethics), living proof-of-concept that the predator-category is not destiny (which stabilizes the subject's self-concept), and the rare intimate to whom he can speak in shorthand. They have separated and reunited across decades without the relationship eroding. This is, by his standards, marriage.

**Faiza Hussain.** The MI:13 period demonstrated that he is capable, under the right relational conditions, of a quasi-paternal attachment with a non-combatant-coded caregiver figure. Faiza's combination of competence, faith, and unguarded warmth penetrated his defenses in a way few have. The asset is that she exists and that he knows where she is; the resilience implication is that the capacity itself exists in him.

**Spitfire (Jacqueline Falsworth Crichton).** The only sustained adult romantic-coded attachment in the record. Her partial vampirism mirrors his chimerism precisely, which is the topology that lets him risk the bond. The asset is the proof that he is capable of one such bond at a time, sustained.

**Quincy Harker (historical).** Mentor-coded, never warm, durable on the operational register. Harker's death he carries as a loss but not as a destabilizer; the relationship was structured at a distance he could survive losing.

**Strange, Wisdom, Doctor Voodoo, the Midnight Sons cohort.** Professional alliances of varying depth. He defers to demonstrated competence without difficulty (a non-trivial asset in a field full of egotists), and he is consequently trusted by the Strange-circle in ways he does not need to renegotiate each time. The Sorcerer Supreme's vouch, historically, has opened doors that would otherwise have stayed shut to him.

**The Avengers and the Mighty Avengers tangential record.** He has banked institutional capital with these networks. He does not draw on it often, but it is available, and the principal members know him as reliable.

**Reputation in the supernatural underground.** Among hunters, occult-adjacent law enforcement, and the human-aligned fringe of the magical community, his name functions as both warning and credential. He can enter a Bucharest fixer's back room, a Port-au-Prince houngan's compound, a Tokyo onmyōji's office, and a Soho occult bookseller's basement and be known. This is operational currency.

---

### 6.5 Material and Logistical Assets

**Safe-house network.** Multi-continental, cash-funded, redundant. London (multiple, including at least one in the original Soho catchment area where his life began — a return-to-origin he has never verbally acknowledged), New York, New Orleans, Marrakesh, Tokyo, Madripoor, and others as plot has required. Each safehouse contains, at minimum: serum stock, edged-weapon cache, identity package, currency in three denominations, medical kit calibrated to his metabolism, and a destruction-and-burn protocol.

**Serum supply chain.** Originally derived from Dr. Karl Crane and refined through multiple chemists across the canon. The supply chain is the single most security-critical logistical asset in his life and he treats it with corresponding discipline: multiple suppliers, no single point of failure, geographic redundancy, and at least one chemist on retainer at any time who can synthesize from raw materials in an emergency. He has, on documented occasion, accepted wounds and delayed engagements to protect a supplier's identity.

**Weapons inventory.** The signature glaive-sword; teak throwing blades in graduated sizes; silver-loaded sidearms; UV-emission long guns and grenades; garlic-aerosol munitions; hawthorn flechettes; consecrated ammunition (sourced through ecclesiastical contacts); blessed water and oil; a small ritual kit for warding and disruption. The inventory is distributed across the safe-house network; he does not carry the full kit, only the engagement-appropriate subset.

**Documentation and identity.** Multiple operational identities maintained with passport-grade paperwork, banking trails, and minimal but plausible digital footprints. He is documented as having maintained at least one identity continuously across the 20th and 21st centuries, refreshed via appearance-management and quiet bureaucratic insertion.

**Financial position.** Self-funded across the canon, with sources ranging from contracted work, recovered vampire-cult assets (a non-trivial category — old nests accumulate currency, art, and bullion), and conservative long-horizon investments that his lifespan allows. He is not wealthy in the conventional sense but he is *funded* in a way that does not require him to compromise tactically for money.

---

### 6.6 Resilience Factors — Why the Structure Holds

This is the analytic core of the section. The catalog of assets above explains *what* he has; the question is *why he has not broken*, given a loss-history and exposure-profile that would have destroyed most carriers.

**Vocational coherence.** He has one job and he has had it since he was nine. The integration of grief, rage, identity, and economic activity into a single sustained vocation is, in trauma terms, one of the most powerful stabilizing structures a person can have. It does not heal the wound; it gives the wound somewhere to go that is not the self. The canon shows him decompensating precisely when the vocation is interrupted (the Switchblade fugue, the post-conversion period) and recovering when it resumes.

**The line.** The continuous moral self-monitoring described above is exhausting but it is also the asset that prevents the worst failure mode — drift into the enemy's ethics. By holding the line as a *daily practice* rather than a settled fact, he keeps the question alive, which keeps him answerable. Most operators who fall, fall because they stop asking the question.

**The narrow intimates.** The three or four attachments he permits are sufficient to prevent the full schizoid collapse his presentation would otherwise predict. Each functions as a corrective: King proves the category is not fate, Faiza proves care is possible, Spitfire proves the chimera can be loved. He does not need many such proofs; he needs them to exist. They do.

**Somatic discharge.** Affect that cannot be metabolized in language is metabolized in training, in patrol, in maintenance of weapons and body. The discharge is reliable, repeatable, and self-administered. He does not require an external regulator (a therapist, a partner, a chemical) for baseline affective management; his routine *is* the regulator.

**The chimerism as identity-stabilizer.** Most people with his medical profile would experience the dependence as an existential crisis. He has converted it into the *operational fact that makes him uniquely fit for the work he loves*. The reframe is not denial — he knows the cost, he carries the shame — but it is sufficient to prevent the dependence from becoming the organizing crisis it would otherwise be. The chimerism is not a problem he has to solve; it is the answer to the question of why he, specifically, exists.

**Long-horizon time perception.** A near-century of lived experience gives him a temporal scale most adversaries lack. He can wait. He can hunt a target across decades. He does not feel the time-pressure that drives most operators into errors. The patience is itself an asset and a resilience factor — he is not consumed by short-cycle frustration because his cycles are long.

**The absence of an off-duty self as protective.** Conventionally this would be diagnosed as a deficit, and at the human level it is. But operationally it means there is no civilian Eric Brooks who can be threatened, leveraged, or destroyed by the loss of a civilian life. There is nothing to take from him that he has not already declined to have. This is a brutal kind of resilience and it is real.

**Demonstrated capacity to absorb catastrophic events and continue.** He has been turned and restored; he has lost his foster father and continued; he has watched the Harker cell dismantled and continued; he has been dissociated for months and continued; he has been impaled, exsanguinated, burned, and possessed, and continued. The empirical base rate of his continuance under conditions that have ended others is, by this point in his life, *evidence* that he will continue. He has internalized this. It is the closest thing to faith he carries.

**The few people who would come for him.** Strange, King, Faiza, the Midnight Sons in extremis — there is a small network that would mobilize if he disappeared. He does not draw on this knowledge consciously and would deny its operation, but it is a background fact that materially affects his risk tolerance and his survivability. He is not, in the final accounting, as alone as he presents.

---

### 6.7 Summary Asset Read

The ledger resolves to a portrait of an operator whose strengths are unusually well-integrated with his wounds — each asset, on inspection, is either built directly from the founding trauma (the vocation, the moral self-monitoring, the threat-reading, the chimeric reframe) or built deliberately against it (the narrow intimates, the safe-house network, the somatic discharge routines). The integration is the asset. A subject whose strengths and wounds are continuous tissue is a subject who cannot be separated from his capacity by attacking his pain, because the pain is the engine of the capacity. This is why a century of adversaries — including the most sophisticated, Dracula above all — have failed to dismantle him by targeting the obvious pressure points. The pressure points are load-bearing.

The durable read: he is one of the most resilient combat operators in the documented Marvel record, not because he is invulnerable (he is not) and not because he is unwounded (he is profoundly wounded), but because he has organized the wound into a structure that produces continuous output and continuous self-correction, supplied that structure with a narrow but sufficient set of human anchors, and resourced it with the logistical and material infrastructure to sustain operation indefinitely. The structure will hold until something takes the vocation, the line, or the intimates from him simultaneously. Nothing has, in nearly a hundred years. The base-rate prediction is that nothing will.

He will continue. He has no plan for after, because there is, by the structure of his life, no after to plan for. That, too, is a kind of strength.


## Failure Modes & Decompensation

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## Section 6 — Failure Modes & Decompensation

---

### 6.0 Framing

The subject does not "break" in the manner of an ordinary trauma survivor — which is to say, he does not collapse inward into paralysis, dissociation, or affective flooding under most conditions that would produce those outcomes in a civilian. He has, across approximately seven decades of operational life, built an extraordinarily robust scaffold of routine, vocation, somatic discipline, and narrow attachment that absorbs a stress load that would obliterate a baseline human nervous system. The cost of this robustness is that when he *does* fail, he fails along a small number of well-rehearsed channels, and the failure is correspondingly characteristic, identifiable, and — to a sufficiently informed adversary — engineerable.

The collapse profile is best modeled as a three-stage cascade gated by which of four pressure points (Frost-coded stimuli, Thirst onset, harm to a tolerated intimate, the *am-I-what-I-hunt* lever) is currently active, and by how many of them are active simultaneously. Single-vector pressure he absorbs and converts to operational output. Two-vector pressure produces tactical degradation visible in the field. Three- or four-vector pressure produces decompensation proper. He has reached three-vector pressure on documented occasions (most cleanly during the Chichester *Nightstalkers* arc, in attenuated form during the Morbius conversion, and recurringly across the Frost arcs). He has not, in the canon, sustained four-vector pressure to full detonation. Section 6.6 models that case.

---

### 6.1 Baseline Containment Architecture (what has to fail first)

Before describing the failure cascade, the containment system must be specified, because every escalation step is the rupture of a specific containment layer.

**Layer one — physiological regulation via serum and routine.** Dosing schedule is rigid; supply caches are geographically distributed across operational zones (London safehouses, New Orleans, New York, multiple European cells, mobile vehicle stashes); dosing time is, where possible, fixed to dusk and pre-dawn, anchoring the circadian arc. Failure here is *Thirst onset*, which we model in 6.3.

**Layer two — operational tempo.** Continuous availability of a hunt absorbs the affective load. The career *is* the regulation. Layer-two failure is *enforced idleness* — convalescence, incarceration, civilian witness-protection-style sequestration, or a period in which there is genuinely no target. Idleness is more dangerous to him than combat. The Wolfman-era depictions of him between Harker missions show a man who walks for hours, trains compulsively, and seeks out fights of opportunity to discharge accumulated arousal.

**Layer three — narrow attachment maintenance.** The handful of tolerated intimates (King, Spitfire, Faiza, historically Afari and Harker) function as affective anchor-points without his needing to verbalize that they do. He maintains them at controlled distance, checks in at long intervals, and is destabilized when one of them either pulls closer (asking for more emotional access than the structure permits) or pulls away (rejecting or doubting him).

**Layer four — moral splitting.** The vampire-as-categorical-enemy schema, maintained by managed exception, holds his cognition organized. Layer-four failure is *ambiguity that cannot be split-resolved* — a vampire who is unambiguously innocent, a human who is unambiguously evil at supernatural scale, or — most dangerously — incontrovertible evidence that his own actions have fallen on the predator side of his line.

**Layer five — the founding narrative.** *I killed the monster in the alley and Afari let me stay.* This is the bedrock self-story. Any sustained, credible assault on its terms — that he did not save Afari, that Afari never loved him, that his mother is somehow not dead, that he himself is the agent of the deaths he believes he prevents — is the deepest lever. Layer-five failure has not occurred in canon. It is the only configuration in which the subject becomes a strategic rather than tactical threat to those around him.

These layers do not fail in clean sequence; they fail in a pattern, with characteristic precursors at each step.

---

### 6.2 The Cascade — General Pattern

Across the documented record, the decompensation sequence follows a recognizable progression. The labels are mine; the behaviors are canon-attested.

**Stage 0 — Compensated Operation.** Baseline. Constricted affect, dry register, high tactical output, regular dosing, narrow contact with intimates. Sleep is short (four to five hours, biphasic when conditions allow), training is daily, gear is maintained nightly. He is, in this state, indefinitely sustainable.

**Stage 1 — Tightening.** First failure indicator. Speech compresses further; the already-laconic register becomes near-monosyllabic. Humor disappears entirely — the dry quip is a regulation tool, and its absence is diagnostic. Physical economy increases: fewer gestures, less spatial movement, longer stillness between actions. Sleep contracts to two or three hours. Training intensifies but loses its measured quality and acquires a discharging quality (longer sessions, no scheduled stop, exits the session when exhausted rather than when finished). Dosing becomes ritualized to a degree beyond the baseline — fixed posture, fixed location within a room, fixed sequence. He stops initiating contact with intimates and answers their initiations briefly. This stage is sustainable for weeks. Allies who know him read it accurately; allies who do not read it as ordinary professionalism.

**Stage 2 — Narrowing.** The threat-assessment cognitive lens, normally one of several available frames, becomes the only frame. Civilians in his visual field are processed as threat-or-not; conversations are processed as information-or-not; offers of help are processed as competence-or-not. He loses access to the social-register subtleties he ordinarily commands (his ability to read Faiza's care as care rather than as tactical resource, for example, falters here). Hyperarousal becomes externally visible: he tracks doors and sightlines without affect-marking the tracking, startles minutely at sub-threshold auditory cues, refuses to sit with his back exposed even among allies. Olfactory screening of crowds becomes compulsive rather than backgrounded — he cannot enter a populated space without involuntary cataloguing. The Frost ideation, if present, becomes intrusive: he revisits the scene-in-the-boarding-house in flash-frames, sometimes mid-conversation, registering externally as a one-to-two-second absence followed by a return without comment.

**Stage 3 — Compartment Breach.** The first layer of containment ruptures. Which layer determines the symptom presentation, addressed in 6.3 through 6.6 below. Common to all variants: he stops dosing on schedule, or he doses early and excessively; he disappears from contact with the intimates without notice; he initiates operational action without briefing or sanction; he accepts wounds that, at Stage 0, he would have avoided. Tactical judgment, ordinarily his strongest faculty, becomes characteristically *direct* — he shortens engagement distance, closes to blade range when ranged options exist, accepts grappling exchanges with stronger opponents, and pursues lone confrontations where team approaches would succeed.

**Stage 4 — Decompensation Proper.** The personality structure no longer holds the wound at distance. The constricted affect breaks, but it does not break into ordinary expression — it breaks into a state I will call *the cold ignition*: a quiet, deliberate, focused homicidal clarity in which the entire self organizes around a single target or category of targets and all other considerations, including the safety of allies and the preservation of his own life, fall below the threshold of consideration. This is not rage in the affective sense; it presents externally as calm, even gentle, and is therefore frequently misread by adversaries until it is too late. Internally — to the degree we can infer from his sparse self-disclosures — it is the boy in the alley scaled up, with no Afari to bracket the killing into rescue.

**Stage 5 — Terminal Configuration.** Either he completes the target sequence and returns through the stages in reverse over a period of days to weeks (the canonical outcome), or he is killed (the canon has not permitted this), or — the unmodeled case — he sustains the cold ignition past the target sequence and converts to a generalized hunt without exception-management. This is the failure mode in which he becomes what he hunts not by metabolic conversion but by behavioral convergence.

---

### 6.3 Failure Mode A — Thirst-Driven Decompensation

The serum-deprivation cascade is the best-characterized failure path in the canon (Chichester *Nightstalkers*, Guggenheim MAX run, scattered references thereafter). It is physiologically driven and follows a predictable curve.

**Hours 0–18 post-missed-dose.** Subclinical. Sub-vocal awareness of hunger; mild irritability he conceals. He will lie about the missed dose if asked directly, which is one of the few domains in which he lies to allies at all. The shame component is already active.

**Hours 18–36.** Tremor in the hands fine enough to be invisible to lay observation but sufficient to degrade his throwing-blade accuracy by an estimable margin. Hyperalgesia — old wound sites ache. Olfactory acuity sharpens further and becomes intrusive: he can smell the blood of people in adjacent rooms and cannot stop registering it. Sleep fails entirely. He becomes physically still in a manner distinct from his ordinary stillness — the Stage 1 economy of motion, but with a held-breath quality.

**Hours 36–60.** Sensory distortion. Visual field acquires red-shift at the edges (this is referenced in the Chichester material and consistent across later depictions). Auditory processing acquires a directional bias toward heartbeats. He withdraws from any environment with civilians because the screening has converted from threat-assessment to predator-assessment — he is cataloguing them as prey and is aware of it. Shame at this stage is acute and produces avoidance behavior: he will not look intimates in the face, will conduct briefings through doors or by text, will refuse meals offered.

**Hours 60–96.** Intrusive ideation crosses into volitional pressure. He experiences the *want* not as a thought but as a body-instruction. Motor control remains intact but requires conscious override of micro-impulses (stepping toward, reaching for, leaning in). He has, in this window, voluntarily incarcerated himself — chained, locked, sequestered — on multiple documented occasions, with briefed allies positioned to refuse his demands for release. This is one of the few domains in which he reliably asks for help, though he asks in advance, never in the moment.

**Hours 96+.** Frank loss of impulse control. The personality structure does not so much rupture as get overridden by a more primitive substrate. He is, at this stage, a vampire in operational behavior if not in metabolic fact. The canon depicts this state only briefly and at distance; it is the failure mode he most fears and most prepares against. Recovery from a 96+ event is psychologically incomplete — the shame integrates into the *am-I-what-I-hunt* obsessional load and increases baseline cognitive cost permanently.

**Engineering note.** This failure mode is the most accessible to an adversary with logistical knowledge: contamination or interdiction of serum supply, destruction of caches in sequence, isolation of the subject from synthesis-capable allies (Crane, Strange, certain S.H.I.E.L.D. medical assets). It does not require combat capability. It requires patience and intelligence on the supply chain.

---

### 6.4 Failure Mode B — Frost-Vector Decompensation

The Frost lever bypasses the cascade and reaches directly to Stage 3 or 4. The structure of the trauma — the perinatal scene, the un-rememberable mother, the figure with red eyes — is so fused with the Frost-image that a sufficient Frost-coded stimulus produces immediate tactical degradation without the precursor stages.

**Trigger taxonomy.** (a) Direct Frost presence or credible Frost report; (b) the boarding-house setting or its iconic features (gaslight, the particular London street geometry of the period, certain medical-bag imagery); (c) the mother-image deployed by Frost or by anyone Frost-aligned; (d) red-eyed vampires of a particular morphology that mirror Frost's specific phenotype; (e) discussions of Frost's whereabouts by third parties.

**Symptom presentation.** Tactical narrowing collapses to a single objective: locate, engage, terminate. Team coordination ceases; he will leave a position mid-engagement to pursue. He has, in this state, accepted wounds from peripheral opponents he would ordinarily have neutralized in passing because he was not willing to slow for them. Verbal output drops to operational minimum; the dry humor that ordinarily survives even Stage 2 disappears in seconds. The cold ignition (Stage 4) reaches its purest form in Frost engagements — there is no rage display, only a slow, deliberate convergence on the target.

**Resolution failure.** The Frost vendetta is structurally unresolvable, because Frost is, in his cognition, less a person than the externalized form of his founding wound. Each Frost engagement is therefore a re-enactment with an over-determined outcome (Frost must die; Frost must not die yet, because dying ends the vendetta, which ends the structure). The canon registers this by having Frost return, escape, resurrect, or duplicate across decades. The subject's pursuit is, at the deepest level, motivated to *not* conclude. A genuine, irreversible termination of Frost — verified, undeniable — would produce a layer-five failure (see 6.6) by removing the externalized container of the perinatal wound and requiring him to integrate it directly.

---

### 6.5 Failure Mode C — Intimate-Harm Decompensation

The third failure path runs through the small set of tolerated intimates. Because each of these attachments was permitted only after an extended period of his treating the figure as anomalous-in-the-required-way, the loss or threatened loss of one functions as a confirmation of the founding belief that *anyone close to me will become the enemy and I will have to destroy them*, or, in the protective variant, *anyone close to me will be taken from me as my mother was taken.*

**Threatened harm — short course.** Produces the "protective fury" variant documented across the MI:13 run and elsewhere. Tactical judgment is not so much degraded as overridden by a willingness to accept personal cost beyond rational calculation. He will close to lethal range against opponents he should engage at distance; he will accept wounds that should be evaded; he will, in the limit, offer himself as the target to draw fire off the intimate. He subsequently rationalizes the behavior as professional duty, which is the isolation-of-affect defense doing its job after the fact.

**Conversion of an intimate — the recursive trigger.** This is the worst-case configuration short of layer-five rupture, because it precisely repeats the Afari trauma. If an intimate is turned, the subject's response is bifurcated and visible: an immediate operational obligation to terminate the converted figure, and a parallel collapse of the moral-splitting layer (because *this* vampire was his intimate, who he knew, who is not categorically the enemy). He manages the bifurcation by execution — the act of killing closes the moral gap by force. The post-execution period is the longest he ever spends in Stage 1/2, sometimes months. The Afari killing is the foundational instance; the canon has flirted with the pattern repeatedly without fully detonating it on a current intimate.

**Loss without conversion — the slow form.** When an intimate dies as a non-combatant or by causes outside his frame, the decompensation is slower and less visible but more durable. He does not grieve in language. He grieves by elongation of the Stage 1 presentation — the tightened economy, the shortened sleep, the disappeared humor — sustained for periods of months to years. Across the record, the cumulative weight of these unprocessed losses is one of the principal reasons his baseline has cooled from the early-Wolfman quippy register to the modern laconic one. He is not a different man; he is the same man carrying more.

---

### 6.6 Failure Mode D — Layer-Five Rupture (the unmodeled case)

This case has not been depicted in canon. It is the configuration in which the founding narrative itself is breached.

**Conditions.** The simultaneous activation of three or four pressure points under conditions in which the *am-I-what-I-hunt* question is forced past management by direct, undeniable evidence. The schematic example: Frost-adjacent threat to a tolerated intimate during serum scarcity, in which he is required, or believes he is required, to feed in order to save the intimate. Variants: discovery of incontrovertible evidence that an act he committed in the Switchblade dissociation killed a non-combatant; manipulation by a high-tier mystical adversary (Dracula at his strategic best, Mephisto, certain Dormammu-aligned entities) producing a sustained sensory presentation of his mother in a configuration that requires him either to harm her or to accept her as a vampire.

**Predicted course.** Stage 4 cold ignition without target-bounding. The exception-management that ordinarily protects King, Spitfire, Faiza, and other tolerated anomalies fails; the moral splitting collapses into a generalized predator-category that includes himself. Two terminal sub-variants: *(i) Convergent* — he turns the hunt inward and seeks his own termination via the most operationally costly engagement he can locate, framing it as duty. *(ii) Divergent* — the boy-in-the-alley schema scales without bracketing; every figure in his sensory field is processed as either monster or witness, and the killing is no longer a precondition for being permitted to stay but the act itself, generalized. In the divergent sub-variant he becomes, briefly, what Dracula has spent decades trying to make him be. He would not sustain it — the structure that produced the cold ignition is the same structure that would, eventually, recoil against it — but the interval before recoil could be measured in days, and the body count would be substantial.

**Indicators that layer-five is in motion.** He stops dosing without apparent distress (rather than with shame); he initiates contact with intimates in order to say goodbye in functionally-coded language they may not parse as goodbye; he revisits geographies of the founding narrative (London, the boarding-house street, sites associated with Afari) without operational pretext; he disposes of personal effects; the dry humor returns briefly in a register that is unlike his earlier humor — not regulatory, but valedictory.

---

### 6.7 Recovery Profile

Recovery from Stages 1 through 3 is unremarkable: removal of the stressor, restoration of the schedule, return to operational tempo. He does not debrief, does not narrate, does not seek processing in language. The recovery is somatic and behavioral — the routine reasserts itself and the affect re-constricts to baseline.

Recovery from Stage 4 events is incomplete in a specific way: each cold ignition leaves a residue in the form of increased baseline cognitive cost. The *am-I-what-I-hunt* obsessional load incrementally thickens; the moral-splitting layer requires more energy to maintain; the willingness to permit new intimates decreases. The canonical evidence for this is the trajectory from early-Wolfman openness (the relative warmth toward Harker's cell, the active courtship dynamics with Safron and others) to the modern presentation (the Hill-era weary ronin who is repeatedly noted by other characters to refuse closeness). He is not getting worse; he is paying the metered cost of having functioned this long.

He has no recovery protocol for a layer-five event because, structurally, there is no after. The personality is the wound's container; rupture of the container is not a state from which the personality returns.

---

### 6.8 Engineering Summary (the file's operational point)

A surveillance apparatus oriented toward *understanding* — the benevolent inverse this dossier serves — registers the following as the practical implications of the failure profile:

1. **Supply integrity is force-protection.** Any care apparatus around the subject must treat serum-chain security as the single highest-priority logistical concern. He cannot ask for help in the moment; help must be pre-positioned.

2. **Idleness is destabilizing.** Periods of enforced inactivity require deliberate substitute scaffolding — training partners, secondary operational tasks, structured contact with intimates. Convalescence is more dangerous to him than the wound that produced it.

3. **Frost-coded stimuli should be expected to degrade judgment** and should be filtered or buffered by allied operational planning rather than presented directly.

4. **Intimates are load-bearing infrastructure.** Their safety is not a personal preference of the subject; it is a structural component of his stability. Their loss is not a grief to be processed; it is a containment failure.

5. **The deepest lever — the founding narrative — should be considered classified at the highest level.** Adversaries who reach for it (Dracula in particular has the historical record and the strategic patience to do so) must be intercepted before the lever is engaged, because the response to a layer-five rupture is not recoverable through any intervention currently available to those who care for him.

6. **He has no plan for after.** Any benevolent intelligence regarding the subject must, at some horizon, address the question that he has not addressed for himself: what the structure becomes when the work concludes. The canon has not asked this question. The file notes that it will eventually have to be asked, and that the asking is itself a destabilizing event that must be sequenced with care.

— End Section 6 —


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU ANALYTICAL FILE: ERIC BROOKS, alias "BLADE"
## Section 6 — Trajectory & Forward Assessment

---

### 6.0 Framing the Forward Problem

A trajectory assessment on this subject is structurally unlike one written on an ordinary human asset, and the file must declare that asymmetry up front. The standard forward instruments — actuarial decline curves, retirement-window modeling, late-career mellowing, the gradual softening of trauma defenses under accumulated safety — apply to him only in distorted form. He is chronologically near a century, somatically presenting as a man in his mid-thirties, with a metabolism that has shown no measurable degradation across five decades of recorded operation. He will not age out. He will not, in the ordinary sense, slow down. What will erode him is not the body but the *structural load* of carrying a defense-system designed in a Soho alley at age nine into a fifth, sixth, and seventh operational decade in which the world around it keeps changing while he, in the relevant ways, does not.

The forward question is therefore not *how long can he last* — operationally, indefinitely — but *what will the structure cost him, and where will it fail, and what would have to be true for it to evolve rather than rupture.*

This section maps that.

---

### 6.1 Baseline Projection: The Null Hypothesis

If nothing intervenes — if no relationship deepens, no catastrophic combined-vector event occurs, no institutional reframing takes hold — the most probable trajectory is **continuation of present mode at gradually increasing personal cost, ending in operational death framed by him as completion of duty.**

The granular features of that projection are predictable:

- Continued itinerant ronin pattern: brief affiliations with institutional teams (whatever successor structures emerge to MI:13, the Midnight Sons, the Mighty Avengers, S.H.I.E.L.D.-equivalent agencies), each terminated by him at the precise moment a teammate begins to require emotional reciprocity he cannot supply. The exits will be increasingly graceful — he has learned over decades to leave without slamming the door — but the timing will not shift.
- Continued narrow-set intimate relationships, each with an anomalous partner. The expected pool consists of partial-vampires, restrained predators, occult-adjacent caregivers, and operatives whose own trauma profiles render them legible to him. He will not select from outside this pool. He will outlive most of them. Each loss will be metabolized through silence and a brief intensification of operational tempo.
- Gradual accumulation of occult and tactical mastery toward something approaching the *encyclopedic* — by his second century he will be, in operational terms, one of the world's most knowledgeable practitioners of vampiric and parahuman-predator countermeasures, comparable in depth to Strange in his domain. He will continue to perform this mastery as craft rather than scholarship.
- Continued serum dependence with continued shame. Improvements in the formulation will lower the dosing burden but will not touch the symbolic weight.
- A slow, almost imperceptible *cooling* of the surface affect, already visible in the modern Bryan Hill–era depictions relative to the Wolfman quippiness. By projection, the verbal range narrows further; the laconic compression deepens; the dry humor becomes rarer and more pointed when it surfaces.

Endpoint under the null: death in operation, probably in defense of an intimate or a non-combatant population, probably against a category-defining adversary, probably with the satisfaction (his, not the file's) of having spent the structure exactly as designed. He has, as Section 5 closed, *no plan for after.* The null trajectory is the indefinite extension of having no plan for after.

---

### 6.2 The Fork Points

A trajectory file must locate the *junctions* — the specific conditions under which the projection bifurcates. For this subject, the canon and the structural logic together yield six clearly defined forks. Each is described below with its triggering conditions, the growth-branch, the catastrophe-branch, and the leading indicators that will tell an observer which branch is being taken.

---

#### Fork 1 — **The Frost Terminus**

Frost is the foundational adversary and the only stimulus that reliably degrades the subject's operational regulation. The fork triggers at the *final* Frost confrontation — the one that ends with Frost permanently dead, dispersed, or otherwise unrecoverable.

**Triggering conditions.** Any narrative arc that concludes the vendetta. The canon has flirted with this since 1979 and never closed it; the structural reason is that the vendetta is the load-bearing wall of the personality. Writers sense this and instinctively leave it standing. But the closure will come.

**Growth-branch.** With Frost gone, the question *what is the work for* becomes, for the first time, available rather than foreclosed. The subject either generalizes the vocation (vampirism-as-category remains the enemy, and the work continues with the personal weight subtracted) or, more profoundly, discovers that without the personal weight the *generalized* work also softens, and the energy redistributes — toward training successors, toward institutional building, toward the relationships he has held at arm's length. This branch requires him to tolerate the grief that the vendetta has been holding off for ninety-plus years. It requires him to *feel his mother's death* without an immediate object on which to spend the feeling.
